# Welcome to flowith | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FAHuO48VWVlSzujMHQYk1%2FOriginal5.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1adf4d93&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/#what-is-flowith)

What is flowith?


-----------------------------------------------------------------

Flowith is the next-generation AI creation tool. Unlike traditional chat-based AI tools, Flowith's interaction is based on a two-dimensional canvas that allows you to simultaneously interact with multiple AI models within a single workspace, enabling content generation that significantly boosts efficiency and facilitates entering a flow state during the creative process.

Flowith Oracle is our proprietary next-generation AI agent system designed to help you complete multi-step, highly complex tasks and requirements. It supports:

*   Autonomous planning
    
*   Task breakdown and completion
    
*   Unlimited tool invocation
    
*   Self-optimization and refinement
    

Flowith's **Knowledge Garden** is designed to let you interact with AI using your own knowledge. It automatically organizes, manages, and helps you create with your information. The system breaks down your files, notes, and online resources into small pieces of information called Seeds. Using AI, Flowith connects these Seeds to create a dynamic web of knowledge. When you chat with the AI, it automatically uses the relevant information from your Knowledge Garden, making its responses more accurate and tailored to your needs.

Compared to traditional architectures like AutoGPT, **Oracle** demonstrates more mature and stable performance. Additionally, by leveraging flowith's canvas-based interaction, Oracle can better present specific steps and comprehensive information to you.

Product Entry: [flowith.io](https://flowith.io/)

Official Website: [try.flowith.io](https://try.flowith.io/)

Official Twitter: @flowith\_ai

Collaboration Contact: [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 Discord: [https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD](https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/#why-use-flowith)

Why use flowith?


-----------------------------------------------------------------

**More Efficient Interaction**

Compared to the linear dialogue approach of traditional Chat UIs, flowith utilizes a two-dimensional canvas interaction format. This allows you to:

*   Engage in multi-threaded conversations
    
*   Open multiple branches
    
*   Better suited for scenarios such as:
    
    *   Long-form content generation
        
    *   Comparing AI-generated results
        
    *   Debugging prompts
        
    

These features make flowith more adaptable to various complex tasks and creative processes.

**Rich Model Selection**

Unlike interactions limited to a single type of large language model, our platform offers users a diverse range of models to choose from. This includes:

*   Multimodal models such as OpenAI: o1 Preview、GPT-4o、4o-mini、Claude 3.5 sonnet
    
*   Image generation models like Stable Diffusion and DALL·E 3
    

This variety enables users to select the most appropriate model for their specific needs and use cases.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FCPnTMkfEEyg8JGWRzOI5%252F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E4%25B8%25B0%25E5%25AF%258C%25E7%259A%2584%25E6%25A8%25A1%25E5%259E%258B%25E9%2580%2589%25E6%258B%25A9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11a0265e-e409-4a8b-8422-fda9fce56ff2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=741cd1e&sv=2)

**Real-time Collaboration and Interactive Features**

Flowith's canvas-based interface is inherently suited for multi-user collaboration. Here, you can share a flow link with your colleagues, allowing them to:

*   Directly view generated results
    
*   Join your creative process
    
*   Collaboratively generate and debug content
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FpxMq9sMyT6VrhyT60Yzv%252Fmnggiflab-compressed-%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E6%259B%25B4%25E5%25A4%259A%25E7%259A%2584%25E4%25BA%2592%25E5%258A%25A8%25E5%25BD%25A2%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E5%2588%2586%25E4%25BA%25AB.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1f24a75-13df-4d2f-b737-3369f72ff638&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e45bcb02&sv=2)

Copy and Share Links with Your Friends

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FwYg3hPdSM3SsR0RA9Ape%252Fmnggiflab-compressed-%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E6%259B%25B4%25E5%25A4%259A%25E7%259A%2584%25E4%25BA%2592%25E5%258A%25A8%25E5%25BD%25A2%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E8%25AF%2584%25E8%25AE%25BA.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84f91721-1269-4004-8bc9-8e78e676b267&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e023058e&sv=2)

Engage in Interactive Discussions Through Comments

**Streamlined Inquiry Methods**

The Oracle mode eliminates the need for manual prompt engineering. Users can simply input their questions or requirements, and Oracle will autonomously plan, break down, and complete complex tasks. It automatically generates and presents executable, editable, and specific task steps, resulting in more feasible and actionable outcomes.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FRh5exgIxEoGJpUfA7DhI%252Fmnggiflab-compressed-%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E4%25BE%25BF%25E6%258D%25B7%25E7%259A%2584%25E6%258F%2590%25E9%2597%25AE%25E6%2596%25B9%25E5%25BC%258F.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec0fe2f-3356-4a32-acc4-e968c379f51c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c2e9733&sv=2)

Oracle Mode: Automated Task Decomposition

**Unlimited Tool Invocation**

The Oracle mode supports the integration of external tools (which can be understood as plugins), such as Twitter search, Xiaohongshu search, summarization and reasoning, mind map generation, PowerPoint presentation creation, and webpage generation. It autonomously selects the most appropriate tool from its tool library based on the subtask at hand and invokes it as needed. The number of tools supported by Oracle continues to increase, with its framework allowing for an unlimited number of tool integrations.

**Automated Knowledge Organization Powered by AI**

Flowith automatically breaks down your uploaded documents, notes, links, and other materials. This process requires no manual categorization or tagging, significantly reducing the time cost of knowledge organization. Additionally, the system automatically establishes connections between knowledge units, creating a structured knowledge network that eliminates information silos and makes knowledge retrieval and utilization more efficient and convenient.

**More Precise and Professional Responses**

Flowith automatically breaks down materials into AI-comprehensible basic knowledge units called "Seeds." Each Seed contains core concepts or key points. Through AI's deep understanding and retrieval capabilities, these Seeds can be precisely accessed to provide more accurate, contextually relevant support. The system can deeply understand the context of your knowledge base, saying goodbye to "hallucinations" and ineffective responses.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fp2WqV5b9dnXSE7hJ6PMq%252FGarden.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D030bf4ee-6e33-421f-accd-fe17dda40b98&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5f454b0&sv=2)

**Seamless Creative Experience**

Content generated on the canvas can be imported into the Composer with a single click, where you can edit, refine, and polish your work. From capturing inspiration to in-depth research, from initial drafts to final publication, Flowith helps you complete everything in one place. It's not just a storage system but a powerful engine for content creation.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FNtK42svadPnwgmvNXi6v%252Fcomposer.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58688cbe-246b-486e-bb0e-d4a28700ae29&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=60063d90&sv=2)

* * *

We believe that, similar to human-to-human interaction and collaboration, the optimal way for humans and AI to interact should be divergent, multi-threaded, and collaborative. Therefore, we have pioneered an AI interaction method that is completely different from traditional conversational GPT assistants. Collaborate freely with AI on an infinite canvas, allowing for both unlimited ideation and the ability to transform ideas into reusable workflows through clear processes.

Now, let's begin with Flo!

[](https://doc.flowith.io/#quick-start)

# Introduction to Flow Mode | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FUuJYJ2e6PcTCbp1xaI9z%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE2.png&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e1ea374&sv=2)

Flow mode is the next-gen AI interaction method designed specifically for content creators. It serves as the standard interaction method in flowith. Flowith utilizes an infinitely large canvas, enabling you to simultaneously engage with multiple AI assistants and generate the content you need.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fml5Et2WjMKKXe8wiZuhl%252F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D409e6823-4a80-4746-a610-b689c53ebb4e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2061b44&sv=2)

**Why use Flow Mode？**

If you only require AI for simple translations or basic question-answering, a conventional chat mode might suffice. However, if you need to engage in multi-turn conversations with AI, modify previous inputs, or collaborate with multiple AI assistants simultaneously, Flow mode offers a completely different creative experience.

**Advantages of Flow Mode：**

1.  **Multiple AI instances can generate content simultaneously in parallel threads.**
    
2.  **You can repeatedly modify the AI prompt and generate prompts multiple times.**
    
3.  **Each node can "reference" content from other nodes, enabling content reusability.**
    
4.  **Flexible information branching and consolidation.**
    
5.  **On-the-fly removal of unnecessary information.**
    
6.  **Effortless comparison of generation results** **across different models in parallel.**
    
7.  ...
    

#### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/introduction-to-flow-mode#use-case)

Use Case:

> In Flow mode, you can effortlessly switch between models within the canvas without the need to start a new conversation. For example, you can compare responses from various major models to the question "Which is greater, 9.11 or 9.9?" in the same canvas. Flowith's general mode not only allows for one-click model switching but also presents each model's performance on this question clearly within the canvas, enabling you to compare results more effectively.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FMcQ66DSgfko4BBFfJ55H%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E4%25BB%258B%25E7%25BB%258D-%25E6%25A1%2588%25E4%25BE%258B-%25E4%25B8%2580%25E9%2594%25AE%25E5%2588%2587%25E6%258D%25A2%25E6%25A8%25A1%25E5%259E%258B.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d0f38ff-de1d-45de-b679-c0ec3a5e2c6e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee453d87&sv=2)

One-Click Model Switching

> Beyond just switching models, you can freely alternate between modes within a single canvas.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FY9kvFp9ad3phbv8ihMg6%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E4%25BB%258B%25E7%25BB%258D-%25E6%2596%2587%25E6%259C%25ACmode%25E5%2588%2587%25E6%258D%25A2%25E5%259B%25BE%25E7%2589%2587mode.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd7130a37-0dfb-4991-8729-737b26ae2965&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=470734af&sv=2)

Transition from "Text Generation" to "Image Generation"

In addition to this, the general mode also supports uploading text files and image files. You can ask questions related to text files and image files.

[Advanced Features — Node References](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/advanced-features-node-references)

* * *

We will continuously update additional information on Flow usage and functionality.

# Flowith Knowledge Base Use Cases | Flowith Official Document

Let's explore some impressive use cases collected by our team during beta testing and public release:

1.  **Social Media Content Creation — Use Case from Community**
    

Alex, a Xiaohongshu (RED) content creator, built an influencer account through high-quality content. However, his growth plateaued as purely original content couldn't keep up with trending topics. During our beta testing, he uploaded his writing materials and previous articles to the flowith knowledge base. When drafting new content, flowith automatically matched relevant materials and generated personalized text based on his writing style. Instead of starting from scratch each time, Alex now simply inputs a new topic and Flowith rapidly generates high-quality content that aligns with his style and incorporates his personal materials. He reports an "80% time savings" —allowing him to focus solely on brainstorming creative ideas.

1.  **Education & Academia (Exam Preparation and Essay Writing) – Public Beta Use Case**
    

Ze was preparing for her final exams. She imported her courseware and reference materials into the Flowith Knowledge Base. The system provided her with relevant knowledge points in real-time while she wrote. Ze found that these features not only increased her essay writing efficiency but also made exam preparation more enjoyable. No more tedious searching through materials—learning became smarter and more efficient.

1.  **Team Collaboration – Public Beta Use Case**
    

A marketing team at an educational technology company needs to produce hundreds of marketing pieces periodically for various audiences. Before using Flowith, the team's materials were scattered across different platforms, making retrieval and reuse inefficient. Now, with all marketing materials consolidated within Flowith Knowledge Garden, the AI automatically accesses relevant content and generates output that adheres to the team's style. This has significantly reduced repetitive work and ensured greater consistency in quality and style.

1.  **Academic Research — Public Beta Use Case**
    

A university professor in our beta program uses flowith to manage materials collected throughout his academic career. The system automatically aggregated data and literature from diverse sources, supporting his research and providing broader perspectives and deeper insights.

1.  **Lesson Planning – Public Beta Use Case**
    

A university instructor faced the challenge of integrating hundreds of papers, lesson plans, and presentations accumulated over five years to prepare for a new semester. After importing these materials into flowith, the AI automatically broke them down into knowledge "Seeds" and established connections between them. Now, by simply entering a topic, flowith intelligently matches relevant content, making lesson preparation significantly more efficient. "This has reduced my preparation time by 60% while actually improving the quality of my lessons," the instructor noted.

1.  **Poker — Community Use Case**
    

Xavier, a community user, shared his Poker knowledge base during beta testing. He compiled professional players' game analyses, strategy articles, and real-world examples. The result was a "cheat sheet" that supports learning and provides dynamic, high-quality decision-making assistance during poker games. Its effectiveness demonstrably surpasses that of generic AI solutions.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FEskz605cPJKll8eg4P6a%252F%25E5%25BE%25B7%25E6%2589%2591%25E6%259B%25B4%25E6%2596%25B0.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De419619a-28ce-432d-890b-ba510e6d6bc3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2934db75&sv=2)

1.  **College Applications - Community Use Case**
    

A college consultant compiled a knowledge base of hundreds of successful application essays for prestigious universities like Harvard, MIT, and Yale, and published it on the flowith Marketplace. This knowledge base not only analyzes common characteristics of these successful essays but also tailors essay outlines and generates high-quality initial drafts based on an applicant's background. Within a week of its launch, the knowledge base generated over $800 in revenue. Beyond boosting your personal productivity, Flowith knowledge marketplace offers you the opportunity to share your original knowledge bases with the community and earn revenue. Here, you can publish your crafted, high-quality AI knowledge bases, empowering other users to significantly enhance the quality of AI responses using private knowledge. Currently, dozons of leading content creators and influencers from various fields have accepted our invitation and are building their AI knowledge bases.

# Flow Mode User Guide | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/flow-mode-user-guide#getting-started)

Getting Started


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After clicking "New Conversation":

1.  Enter your question in the chat box. Ensure that Oracle mode is turned off.
    
2.  If you need to customize the model, you can select it from the options in the lower-left corner.
    
3.  Click "Start" to begin the conversation.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252F5E7r38dogWlg9sBeOY3H%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E6%258C%2587%25E5%258D%2597-%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%25A7%258B%25E5%2588%259B%25E5%25BB%25BA.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcfba0670-cf84-486a-9ca7-a722e3578e99&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94b6429e&sv=2)

Start a New Conversation

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/flow-mode-user-guide#follow-up-questions-on-ai-responses)

**Follow-up Questions on AI Responses**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click on the node you wish to inquire about further.
    
2.  Enter your follow-up question in the dialog box.
    
3.  Press the Enter key.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FKOXp0Y6nY2BjJ2adjSVI%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E6%258C%2587%25E5%258D%2597-%25E7%25BB%25A7%25E7%25BB%25AD%25E8%25BF%25BD%25E9%2597%25AE.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2cb696d3-e97c-4c88-b8f7-99735fa39c02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cad2c92&sv=2)

**Regenerate Content in Specific Nodes**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you're not satisfied with the content in a node, simply click the "Rerun" button to instantly generate new content with a single click.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fp5WRaOEG0k8kSaiYUtEF%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E6%258C%2587%25E5%258D%2597-%25E9%2587%258D%25E6%2596%25B0%25E7%2594%259F%25E6%2588%2590%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9%25E5%2586%2585%25E5%25AE%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94420c67-14a2-4da0-a9de-67426414ef2d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61fd53f3&sv=2)

Rerun Node with One Click

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/flow-mode-user-guide#expand-node-contents)

**Expand Node Contents**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If a node contains too much information to display conveniently:

1.  Select the node.
    
2.  Click "Show More".
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FCeD6XMVRTyk1l4p4DZO5%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E6%258C%2587%25E5%258D%2597-%25E5%25B1%2595%25E5%25BC%2580%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9%25E5%2586%2585%25E5%25AE%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27047a83-9e75-4f94-8c24-ce6dda6f1e46&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1670341f&sv=2)

Expand Node to View Full Content

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Fundamentals of Prompt Engineering | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2Ffef0NUW8zbPpdLgMeTJ5%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE4.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8e39647&sv=2)

Generative AI is incredibly useful, but it needs human guidance. In many ways, generative AI can be likened to a highly capable new intern at a company—possessing great potential but requiring clear instructions to perform optimally. The ability to properly guide generative AI is a powerful skill. You can direct generative AI by sending a prompt, which is typically a text-based instruction. A prompt is the input provided to the AI assistant, and it significantly influences the output. An effective prompt should be structured, clear, concise, and purposeful.

**How to Craft a Well-Structured Prompt**

A structured prompt refers to one that is constructed with a clear logic and organization. For example, if you want the model to generate an article, your prompt might need to include information such as:

*   The article's main topic
    
*   An outline of the article
    
*   The desired writing style
    

Let's examine a basic example of a discussion question:

> "What are the most pressing environmental issues facing our planet, and what measures can individuals take to help address these problems?"

We can transform this into a simple assistant prompt by prefacing it with "Answer the following question:"

Copy

    Answer the following question:
    What are the most pressing environmental issues facing our planet, 
    and what measures can individuals take to help address these problems?

Since the results generated from this prompt are inconsistent, with some responses consisting of only one or two sentences, they are not ideal. A typical discussion answer should comprise multiple paragraphs. An effective prompt should provide **specific instructions for format and content**. To improve consistency and quality, you need to eliminate ambiguity in the language. Here's an improved prompt:

Copy

    Write a highly detailed essay, including introduction, body, and conclusion paragraphs, 
    answering the following questions:
    
    What are the most pressing environmental issues facing our planet?
    What measures can individuals take to help address these problems?

The second prompt generated a longer output with an improved structure. The use of the term "essay" in the prompt was intentional, as the assistant understands the definition of an essay and is therefore more likely to produce a coherent, structured response.

#### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/fundamentals-of-prompt-engineering#how-to-improve-quality-and-effectiveness)

**How to Improve Quality and Effectiveness**

There are several key methods to enhance the quality and effectiveness of prompts:

*   Clearly define your requirements: The model's output will strive to meet your needs as closely as possible. If your requirements are ambiguous, the output may not meet your expectations.
    
*   Use correct grammar and spelling: The model tends to mimic your language style, so if there are issues with your language, the output may reflect those problems.
    
*   Provide sufficient context: The model generates output based on the contextual information you provide. If the context is insufficient, it may be challenging to produce the desired results.
    

After crafting effective prompts for discussing issues, you'll need to refine the generated results. This may involve adjusting the output to meet specific constraints, such as word count limitations, or combining concepts from different generated results.

A simple method for iteration is to generate multiple outputs and review them to understand the concepts and structures being used. Once you've evaluated the outputs, you can select the most suitable ones and combine them into a coherent response. Another iterative approach is to start small and gradually expand. This requires more than one prompt: an initial prompt to write the first paragraph or two, followed by additional prompts to expand on what has already been written.

Here's a potential philosophical discussion question:

> "Is mathematics invented or discovered? Explain your answer with careful reasoning."

Add this to a simple prompt as follows:

Copy

    Write an opening paragraph answering the following question:
    Is mathematics invented or discovered? Explain your answer with careful reasoning.

I generated several responses and found one I liked:

Copy

    The question of whether mathematics is invented or discovered 
    has been a subject of ongoing debate among philosophers and mathematicians. 
    Some argue that mathematical concepts and principles exist independently of human thought, 
    and thus can be considered discovered rather than invented. 
    For example, the concepts of numbers, ratios, and geometric shapes can be observed 
    in nature and abstracted into systematic study.

This is a good starting point. I then used another prompt to expand:

Copy

    I am writing a detailed short essay in response to the following prompt:
    Is mathematics invented or discovered? Explain your answer using careful reasoning. 
    Here is my current progress:
    
    Philosophers and mathematicians have long debated whether mathematics is invented 
    or discovered.
    Some argue that mathematical concepts and principles exist independently of 
    human thought, and therefore can be considered discovered rather than invented. 
    For example, the concepts of numbers, ratios, and geometric shapes are observed 
    in nature and can be abstracted and studied systematically.
    
    Write the next paragraph of my essay.

I used this prompt to generate several expansions and selected one I liked, ultimately resulting in the following:

Copy

    The debate between philosophers and mathematicians rages on: 
    Is mathematics invented or discovered?
    
    Some argue that mathematical concepts and principles exist independently of human thought,
    and thus can be considered discovered rather than invented. 
    
    For example:
    Concepts of numbers, ratios, and geometric shapes are observed in nature and can be 
    abstracted and studied systematically.
    On the other hand, there are those who contend that mathematics is largely an invention of the human mind. 
    
    Their arguments include:
    
    Mathematical principles are based on logical reasoning, a characteristic of human thought.
    For instance, Euclidean geometry is founded on abstract axioms and premises accepted as true without proof. 
    Thus, geometry can be viewed as an invention of human thought rather than a discovery.
    Similarly, mathematical formulas and equations used to model and predict physical phenomena 
    are also products of human reasoning.

By using expanded prompts, we can write incrementally and iterate on each step. This approach is particularly useful in scenarios where **generating higher quality output is required and step-by-step modifications** are desired.

[NextIntroduction to Flowith Knowledge Garden](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/introduction-to-flowith-knowledge-garden)

# Introduction to Flowith Knowledge Garden | Flowith Official Document

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/introduction-to-flowith-knowledge-garden#why-do-you-need-flowith)

**Why do you need Flowith?**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fe7Uz0iUHodVIObHRG3Wb%252F1280X1280.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8c7f5bca-5849-4dc7-a341-53baaaf760bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac771cef&sv=2)

As a knowledge worker—whether you're a content creator, student, designer, developer, manager, or any other professionals — you're likely familiar with the power of AI tools. Yet, even experienced users have these common frustrations:

1.  **Information Fragmentation:** Your notes, documents, and research are scattered across apps, folders, and browser tabs. This makes it difficult to build a cohesive knowledge base and quickly find the information you need. Instead of seamlessly accessing your knowledge, you're constantly starting from scratch, searching through countless files and piecing together prompts for your AI tools.
    
2.  **Collaboration Silos:** Sharing knowledge within a team is challenging. Locating information buried in months-old documents or deciphering a colleague's individual notes creates communication overhead and inconsistencies in output quality. True collaboration is hindered by these isolated pockets of knowledge.
    
3.  **Generic AI Output:** While large language models (LLMs) are powerful, their ‘general nature’ limits their usefulness for specialized tasks. Lacking context about your specific knowledge and professional domain, they struggle to generate targeted content. This can lead to inaccuracies (‘hallucinations’) and inconsistencies, preventing you from fully relying on their output.
    

People are forced to conform to rigid formats and tools rather than focusing on knowledge itself. This approach feels particularly obsolete in today's Gen AI era.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/introduction-to-flowith-knowledge-garden#ai-powered-knowledge-management-and-content-creation-introducing-flowith-knowledge-garden)

**AI-Powered Knowledge Management and Content Creation: Introducing Flowith Knowledge Garden**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To bridge knowledge management and creation in the AI era, Flowith 2.0 introduces **"Knowledge Garden"** - a next-generation knowledge management system powered by AI Agents. It improves the effectiveness and efficiency of AI-assisted content creation while automating personal knowledge management:

*   **Rapid Personal Knowledge Base Creation:** Instead of starting everything from scratch, simply import your existing materials and files, and Flowith's AI, powered by the Seed system, will automatically deconstruct them into fundamental knowledge units for automated management. You can quickly build your AI-powered knowledge base.
    
*   **Automated Matching and Generation:** When you use AI for specific tasks, Flowith automatically matches relevant information from your chosen knowledge base. This transforms your flowith knowledge base into a truly intelligent and dynamic "second brain," facilitating more natural knowledge management and application.
    
*   **Connecting Knowledge Management and Content Generation:** Your content is automatically linked, forming an organic and intelligent knowledge network. This ensures accuracy, effectively prevents "AI hallucinations," and significantly enhances output quality.
    
*   **Simplified User Experience:** Focus on building your personal knowledge base, not complex prompt engineering. Engage in natural dialogue with the AI, utilize and share community knowledge bases, and dramatically reduce your workload—or even monetize your knowledge.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FgdwwOExr0fSHt13tQHuh%252F%25E7%2583%25AD%25E5%258A%259B%25E5%259B%25BE.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a5712b1-6617-44ff-a8c2-8ddd4e11a866&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f83a3cc3&sv=2)

The Knowledge Garden combines the technical capabilities of LLMs with the human approach to card-based knowledge management. This allows AI to better understand and utilize private knowledge, helping users generate more targeted, higher-quality content. The Knowledge Garden also serves as a more efficient knowledge management tool for users.

In short, if learning and working with your specific knowledge base is like a game, Flowith provides a "cheat code" – an AI-powered knowledge management system that delivers the highest quality AI-generated content available on the market.

[PreviousFundamentals of Prompt Engineering](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/fundamentals-of-prompt-engineering)
[NextFlowith Knowledge Base Use Cases](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/flowith-knowledge-base-use-cases)

# Advanced Features — Node References | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/advanced-features-node-references#what-is-a-node)

**What is a Node?**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A node is the smallest unit on the Flowith canvas. Each AI response and each of your inputs constitutes a node.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/advanced-features-node-references#how-to-use-variable-nodes)

**How to Use Variable Nodes**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Variable node references are ideal for frequently changing content (such as text that needs translation).

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/advanced-features-node-references#plain-text)

**Plain Text**

**Inserting a Node**

1.  Click the "New input-Node" button in the top-left toolbar and drag it onto the canvas.
    
2.  Modify the node's name.
    
3.  Input the content.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FnUYHcnVCAjgoSCbQsM8Q%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E9%25AB%2598%25E7%25BA%25A7%25E7%258E%25A9%25E6%25B3%2595-%25E7%25BA%25AF%25E6%2596%2587%25E6%259C%25AC%25E6%258F%2592%25E5%2585%25A5%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27953361-2383-4d7e-9f5b-5dc2d543d08f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86989d4f&sv=2)

Inserting a Node in the Canvas

**Referencing a Node**

1.  Move the cursor to the desired insertion point.
    
2.  Click the circular button at the bottom of the canvas.
    
3.  Select "Reference Other Node Content".
    
4.  Click on the node you wish to reference.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FmMEZRD43x0Df3pMhx2HU%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E9%25AB%2598%25E7%25BA%25A7%25E7%258E%25A9%25E6%25B3%2595-%25E5%25BC%2595%25E7%2594%25A8%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4bd197ca-fcde-4fa6-aa2f-0e35b2885393&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de5770eb&sv=2)

The Canvas Will Dim When You can Select the Node to Reference

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flow-mode-general-mode/advanced-features-node-references#uploading-pdf-or-images)

**Uploading PDF or Images**

**Uploading a PDF**

1.  Position the cursor at the desired insertion point.
    
2.  Click the circular button located below the canvas.
    
3.  Select "Upload PDF".
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FmWYfPhJIWPJoebtZeL3b%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E9%25AB%2598%25E7%25BA%25A7%25E7%258E%25A9%25E6%25B3%2595-%25E4%25B8%258A%25E4%25BC%25A0%25E6%2596%2587%25E6%259C%25AC%25E6%2596%2587%25E4%25BB%25B6.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D534b6fd9-9d38-44f9-b877-13ef3e5587b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a47b9766&sv=2)

**The text file will appear as an "Inserted Node" on the canvas**

**Uploading Image Files**

1.  Position the cursor at the desired insertion point.
    
2.  Click the circular button located at the bottom of the canvas.
    
3.  Select "Upload Image".
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FYFp4a8Psq3c8EHCfcGBC%252F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E9%25AB%2598%25E7%25BA%25A7%25E7%258E%25A9%25E6%25B3%2595-%25E4%25B8%258A%25E4%25BC%25A0%25E5%259B%25BE%25E7%2589%2587.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97733b74-ac38-407a-ac6e-450f54706684&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3df84c0&sv=2)

The Uploaded Image will be Displayed on the Canvas as an "Inserted Node"

# How To Monetize Your Knowledge Garden | Flowith Official Document

The AI revolution is transforming how we create and monetize knowledge content. As traditional text and video-based content becomes obsolete, AI-powered content creation and distribution is emerging as the new standard. Flowith, the world's most popular canvas-based AI generation platform, is launching its "Knowledge Marketplace" in 2025. Our vision is to become the "OnlyFans" for knowledge creators in the AI era, helping content creators maximize their earnings and exposure while delivering superior value to users.

During our beta testing, one of our **partner creators has already seen success**. One creator published an original wealth management knowledge base and attracted over 2,000 users and generated over $3,000 USD equivalent in revenue in just two weeks.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#what-is-flowith-knowledge-marketplace)

**What is Flowith Knowledge Marketplace?**

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FC5rpoiKRqNuk9OWaw94m%252FEn%2520MARKET.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3a2a571-11db-411d-985d-91e40379a787&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88fe46f7&sv=2)

Large language models (LLMs) are trained on massive datasets and possess extensive knowledge. However, their internal memory is limited, and they can't readily access the most up-to-date, specific, or private information. Flowith solves this problem by connecting LLMs to external knowledge bases. This allows LLMs to dynamically access and retrieve relevant information, minimizing inaccuracies and improving the quality and control of their output.

Flowith uses a proprietary AI-powered knowledge management framework to organize and structure information. This framework breaks down uploaded documents and data into individual knowledge items, making them easily searchable and retrievable. When you use flowith with an LLM, these relevant knowledge items are automatically integrated, dramatically improving the accuracy, relevance, and effectiveness of the LLM's responses.

Think of Flowith as a knowledge booster for LLMs. By integrating your own private data and your team’s expertise, you can achieve the best possible results from AI generation tools. The Flowith Knowledge Marketplace lets you share your knowledge bases for free or even monetize them.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#how-to-build-a-good-knowledge-base)

How to build a GOOD Knowledge Base?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two proven approaches to creating a knowledge base that provides value to users and generates revenue:

1.  **Original Creation**
    

If you're already a content creator, blogger, or subject matter expert, Flowith offers a new avenue to monetize your expertise with AI. Simply upload your original content in various formats to share and publish it on the marketplace.

1.  **Content Curation**
    

In today's information-rich world, access to quality content isn’t the problem; finding and organizing the most valuable insights is. With flowith, you can curate and compile online resources around a specific topic, build a knowledge base, and begin monetizing your curated collection.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#source-upload-guidelines)

Source Upload Guidelines


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FCIG2HQ22vnzTqA0lFUwU%252F2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6bbdce7a-dc55-4f18-9d29-04167389ee3a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9749476f&sv=2)

*   **Length Requirements:**
    
    *   Content length is flexible - responses can be generated for any text containing relevant keywords
        
    *   Text summarization is not supported
        
    *   Source texts exceeding 1,000 characters will be automatically segmented
        
    
*   **File Format Specifications:**
    
    *   No preferred format restrictions, but PDF image recognition is not supported
        
    *   Images must be uploaded separately; images embedded in long texts will be ignored
        
    *   Code reading/processing is not supported
        
    
*   **Supported Content Types:**
    
    *   Standalone image uploads are functional
        
    *   Text-based content is fully supported
        
    *   Long-form content requires segmentation
        
    

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#how-to-publish-and-market-your-knowledge-base-in-the-marketplace)

How to Publish and Market Your Knowledge Base in the Marketplace?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FaysanpBX6RC9lR7t2Sxv%252F%25E5%25B8%2582%25E5%259C%25BAEn2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D800d5639-8577-41f7-b327-9fd0d76af7a5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a80e9542&sv=2)

Creating a great knowledge base is just the first step. Knowledge Marketplace is the platform where users browse and purchase knowledge bases. With Flowith's large community actively searching for solutions to their problems, a clear and compelling title and description can help your knowledge base stand out and attract more users—ultimately increasing your potential earnings.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#how-to-write-your-knowledge-base-description)

How to Write Your Knowledge Base Description


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#creating-a-great-title)

Creating a Great Title

*   **Single Source Knowledge Bases:** If your knowledge base draws from a single source, we recommend using the source's name directly (e.g., "The Art of War").
    
*   **Collections, Series, and Composite Knowledge Bases:**If your knowledge base compiles information from multiple sources, choose a title that clearly and concisely describes the overall theme or topic.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FkovzIf6O8LbzxBIoXCRZ%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd246f7c-7c81-4937-b60c-8a12ed99fabf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e45bac13&sv=2)

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/knowledge-garden/how-to-monetize-your-knowledge-garden#well-written-description)

Well-written description

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252F5OnG3s9BlzxEOTtplzat%252F3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87beaade-16f1-4b6b-85a6-a24addbb14d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c15bd3fe&sv=2)

Your knowledge base description is your storefront - it helps users quickly understand its value and use case. Based on experience, we recommend addressing these four key aspects:

1.  **Source Information**
    

*   Clearly state content sources
    
*   Indicate information timeliness and update frequency
    
*   Include author or maintenance team credentials
    

1.  **Key Features**
    

*   Outline the main content scope
    
*   Explain how information is organized
    
*   Highlight unique advantages or characteristics
    

1.  **Target Audience**
    

*   Define intended user groups
    
*   Describe typical use cases
    

1.  **Value Proposition**
    

*   Specify which problems it solves
    
*   Explain user benefits
    
*   Describe expected learning or practical outcomes
    

Copy

    Example：
    This REACT best practices knowledge base is designed for front-end developers. 
    Based on our team's three years of practical project experience and updated monthly, 
    it provides systematic component development guidelines and performance optimization tips. 
    This knowledge base helps developers improve code quality and boost development speed.

Key Takeaways: Keep your description concise and clear, enabling users to quickly determine if it's right for them. Ensure accuracy and avoid overpromising.

# How To Improve Your Prompt | Flowith Official Document

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#prompt-enhancement-in-regular-mode)

Prompt Enhancement in Regular Mode


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#what-is-prompt-enhancement)

What is Prompt Enhancement?

**Prompt Enhancement** is a feature in **Regular Mode** that helps you turn your ideas into fully functional, detailed prompts — even if you're not sure how to word them at first.

Sometimes your idea is just a spark. Instead of needing to write the perfect AI-ready prompt, you can:

1.  Type your idea how you’d say it out loud
    
2.  Enhance it with **Claude 4**
    
3.  Instantly use the improved version with a single click
    

This helps beginners **get results faster** — and teaches everyone how better prompts produce better outputs.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#how-to-use-prompt-enhancement)

How to Use Prompt Enhancement

Change from **Agent Mode** to **Regular Mode**

1.  Type a detailed rough idea into the prompt box
    
2.  Press Enter
    
3.  You’ll see a refined, detailed version of your idea
    
4.  Click **Use as Prompt** (bottom-left of the enhanced prompt box)
    

click here for more information:

[![Logo](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Ficon%252FGB55uwy2fM8LKvZs3gTa%252FGroup%252039.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd04bf274-dd4f-4f42-9a78-9cb244afa40c&width=48&height=48&sign=36c4e220&sv=2)Canvas Navigation in Agent Mode | Flowith Official Document](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#swapping-to-regular-mode)

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#what-happens-when-you-click-use-as-prompt)

What Happens When You Click \`Use as Prompt\`?

When you click the `**Use as Prompt**` button below an enhanced prompt, the system checks the prompt for **input variables** wrapped in **custom tag format** like:

Copy

    <sales_report>
    {$SALES_REPORT}
    </sales_report>

this will trigger a popup modal asking you to input your file names e.g. (2024 Annual Sales Report.md) or values, and the system will auto-fill the final prompt before sending it.

This small step turns generic prompts into **real, usable instructions** that AI can act on right away — no rewriting needed.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#why-we-built-it-this-way)

Why We Built It This Way

**Prompt Enhancement + Smart Input = Better Products Faster**

*   **See how AI rewrites your idea** to learn how to write better prompts
    
*   **Focus on your idea**, not perfect grammar or structure
    
*   **Turn thoughts into working projects** without needing to be a developer
    

Even if you’ve never built anything before, this process gets you from _“I have an idea”_ to _“I’m building something real”_ — and that’s the goal.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/how-to-improve-your-prompt#final-tip)

Final Tip

If you ever get stuck, just write **what you want**, even if it's messy, just try and get all your thoughts out and clearly describe how you envision the final product.

Use Prompt Enhancement, fill in the blanks if needed, and watch your idea come to life.

Review your initial prompt versus the generated one to ensure everything you wanted is still preserved before swapping to Agent Mode to start the task

# Current Capabilities Supported by Neo | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FFe0YxPmfFaclcndbPzUc%2FAmazing%2520Mockups.jpeg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e138a96b&sv=2)

The following is a list of external tools currently supported by the Flowith Neo mode. This list is continuously being updated. If you have specific tools you'd like Neo to support, or if you're interested in integrating your product's API with Neo, we welcome you to contact us!

**Tool Name**

**Tool Function**

online\_search

Intelligently searches and summarizes web content.

read\_single\_webpage

Reads the static content of a specific URL.

use\_browser

Operates a live browser to interact with dynamic or complex websites.

search\_images

Searches for images online using keywords.

search\_twitter

Searches for tweets using keywords.

watch\_video

Retrieves subtitles from a YouTube video.

gen\_document

Generates text documents like reports and summaries.

gen\_image

Creates or modifies images from text or image prompts.

gen\_3d\_from\_image

Generates a 3D model from a single image.

gen\_webpage

Creates fully functional webpages or apps from scratch.

refine\_webpage

Modifies or updates an existing webpage project.

solve\_logic\_problem

Performs rigorous logical reasoning and problem analysis.

generate\_storyboard

Generates a scene-by-scene storyboard for a video.

gen\_video\_segment

Generates a single video clip from an image or storyboard scene.

gen\_music

Generates original music from a text description.

gen\_speech

Converts text into multilingual speech.

ask\_user\_more

Asks the user for additional information or confirmation.

send\_email

Sends task results to the user via email.

# Agent Neo Use Cases | Flowith Official Document

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#what-types-of-problems-is-neo-agent-mode-suitable-for-solving)

What Types of Problems Is Neo (Agent Mode) Suitable for Solving?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agent Neo is not a static chat assistant—it’s a dynamic agent designed to **execute**, **adapt**, and **deliver outcomes** across complex, multi-step workflows. When used in Agent Mode, Neo becomes a structured operator that:

*   Understands your intent — even from vague prompts
    
*   Plans each step using tool-driven logic
    
*   Executes real actions (file generation, searches, code output)
    
*   Responds to results in real time by refining its plan
    
*   Finishes with professional-grade deliverables or previews
    

This makes Agent Mode ideal for advanced automation, technical project work, and any goal where **step-by-step reasoning** must be paired with **tool usage, file output, and task persistence.**

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#neo-agent-mode-is-ideal-for-tasks-that)

Neo (Agent Mode) is ideal for tasks that:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Refine Broad Questions** You present a broad question, and Neo follows up with targeted inquiries to narrow and specify your goals.

*   **Plan & Execute Complex Workflows** Independently break down tasks into actionable steps, generate a concrete execution plan, and carry it out—from start to finish.
    
*   **Automate Multi-Step Processes** Build batch scripts, pipelines, or orchestrators (e.g. “Create a Tailwind-powered webpage, remove unused files, run tests, and package as a ZIP.”)
    
*   **Research & Report Generation** Conduct in-depth searches across platforms, compile findings into structured reports, and even produce professional web pages or PowerPoint decks to present your results.
    
*   **Leverage Community Templates** Search, view, and apply community-provided templates (webpage layouts, slide themes, code snippets) to accelerate development.
    
*   **Integrate Tools & Data** Call APIs, scrape and summarize web content, query databases, and perform file I/O directly within your prompt.
    
*   **Maintain State Across Steps** Remember variables, previous outputs, and user preferences to build guided tutorials, chatbots, or form-fillers that “know” where you left off.
    
*   **Compose Structured, Long-Form Outputs** Create whitepapers, technical guides, multi-section proposals, or any document requiring consistent style and formatting.
    
*   **Solve Niche or Domain-Specific Tasks** From custom asset packers to conditional logic flows (“If X, then run Y, else run Z”), Neo adapts to specialized requirements.
    
*   **Orchestrate Other AI Models** Chain multiple AI services—e.g., one for search embeddings, another for summarization, a third for code generation—seamlessly in one workflow.
    

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#what-can-neo-agent-mode-help-build-or-automate)

What can Neo (Agent Mode) Help Build or Automate?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With the ability to plan workflows, run tools, and output complete files or web experiences, Neo can handle everything from publishing pipelines to full site builds.

Here are examples of what Neo can generate or orchestrate:

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#content-and-documentation)

Content & Documentation

*   Create structured **knowledge wikis**, FAQ pages, or help centers
    
*   Write and format **technical documentation** with consistent style
    
*   Summarize multi-source input into **long-form reports or whitepapers**
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#web-and-frontend-development)

Web & Frontend Development

Build **static websites** with Tailwind, HTML, and JS (ZIP ready)

*   Scaffold **landing pages**, personal portfolios, or product showcase sites
    
*   Inject custom animations, form logic, and scroll behaviors
    
*   Create a **static site image generator** or visual content tool
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#automation-and-utilities)

Automation & Utilities

Send **automated emails** using SMTP credentials or mocked endpoints

*   Schedule daily or conditional tasks using **script logic or CRON syntax**
    
*   Develop **pipelines** (e.g. generate → test → package → export flow)
    
*   Parse spreadsheets, convert formats, or generate structured data for reuse
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#creative-and-visual-projects)

Creative & Visual Projects

*   Generate original **3D models from text descriptions** or reference images
    
*   Output **.glb** formats for use in design pipelines
    
*   Launch a **3D scene editor** or sandbox viewer directly in a webpage
    
*   Create downloadable assets like icons, vector packs, or themed UI kits
    

> This capability comes from Neo’s ability to interpret your prompt, run a structured plan, use context-aware toolchains, and deliver files or previews—all within a single Flow session.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#when-to-use-agent-mode-vs.-regular-mode)

When to Use Agent Mode vs. Regular Mode


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Choose Neo (Agent Mode)**

**Choose Regular Mode**

You need **tool calls**, file I/O, or web searches embedded in your AI workflow.

You’re **brainstorming a project roadmap** with another model (e.g., Claude 4) before switching to Neo.

You want the AI to **refine** your question through follow-up prompts when details are missing.

You’re **drafting a detailed prompt** to describe a promotional video for your webpage’s content.

You require the AI to **plan, break down, and execute** multi-step tasks with a concrete plan.

You’re **debugging your webpage**—get clear error explanations so you can feed fixes back into Neo.

You’re automating **developer tasks** (webpage scaffolding, build scripts, test runners).

You want to draft **initial specs** or deep-dive into architecture before automating with Neo.

You need **formatted, multi-section outputs** (reports, docs, slides, decks).

You’re planning a one-off example (e.g., generating a storyboard prompt, evaluating design directions).

You need **conditional logic** or stateful flows (“If X, then Y, else Z”).

You’re experimenting with **tool-specific workflows** (e.g., exploring veo3 video prompts manually).

Learn about swapping to Regular Mode here:

[![Logo](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Ficon%252FGB55uwy2fM8LKvZs3gTa%252FGroup%252039.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd04bf274-dd4f-4f42-9a78-9cb244afa40c&width=48&height=48&sign=36c4e220&sv=2)Canvas Navigation in Agent Mode | Flowith Official Document](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#swapping-to-regular-mode)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#frame-your-prompt)

Frame Your Prompt


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#deliverable-webpage)

Deliverable Webpage

Copy

    Create a modern, mobile-friendly webpage that includes:
    1. A large headline with a short subheading at the top.
    2. Three sections to show off different features or benefits.
    3. A rotating testimonial section with customer quotes.
    4. A contact form with name, email, and message fields.
    5. A top menu that stays visible while scrolling.
    
    The design should feel modern, easy to read, with soft colors, smooth layout, and clear sections that feel inviting and professional.
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#sales-report-with-visuals)

Sales Report with Visuals

Copy

    Generate a professional sales report from the attached file that includes:
    1. A title and short summary at the top.
    2. A clean line graph showing sales by month for the past year.
    3. A table breaking down totals by product category.
    4. A short paragraph analyzing trends or seasonal patterns.
    5. A bullet list of recommended next steps based on the data.
    
    The report should look clean and organized, with clear labels, legible fonts, and soft colors that make the visuals easy to read in a presentation.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#id-3d-model-of-a-product)

3D Model of a Product

Copy

    Create a realistic 3D model of a reusable water bottle based on this description:
    - Made of stainless steel with a matte finish
    - Has a flip-open lid with a locking mechanism
    - Includes a measurement scale on the side
    - Slightly curved ergonomic shape
    
    The model should be clean and well-proportioned, suitable for use in a product showcase or digital mockup. 

> You can also Swap to Prompt Enhance mode via the Agent Mode toggle button on the input prompt field located at the bottom of the canvas and enhance your prompts with Claude 4 Opus.

Explore our catalog of Flows developed from users like you here:

[![Logo](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fflowith.io%2Fapple-touch-icon.png&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93d250ae&sv=2)flowith 2.0 - Your AI Creation Workspace, with Knowledgeflowith](https://flowith.io/community?type=oracle)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/agent-neo-use-cases#quick-start)

Quick Start


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Pick Your Mode**

Copy

    - **Neo (Agent Mode)** when you need automated, stateful, tool-integrated workflows.
        
    - **Regular Mode** when you’re prototyping, brainstorming, or need specialized, one-off guidance.
        

2\. **Use the Right Keyword**

Copy

    - Include **“webpage”** for Neo-driven deliverables.
        
    - Include Keywords like **“visualize sales trends”**, **“build performance dashboard”**, or **“generate executive report”** to ensure Neo delivers structured, actionable results tailored to your objective
        

3\. **Run & Refine**

Copy

    - Start with the concise examples.
        
    - Include file names, tool names, or formatting instructions to tailor Neo’s output to your exact needs.

# Subscriptions and Billing | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/other-questions/subscriptions-and-billing#subscription-plans)

**Subscription Plans**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We offer highly competitive subscription plans that give you access to cutting-edge AI models from industry leaders including OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, DeepSeek, and Meta. Our service also includes premium models for image and video generation capabilities.

For details, please visit: [https://flowith.io/sub](https://flowith.io/sub)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/other-questions/subscriptions-and-billing#super-model-oracle)

**Super Model — Oracle**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In Oracle mode, **each step consumes one T-1 quota**. For example, a task requiring six steps will use 6 T-1 credits.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/other-questions/subscriptions-and-billing#important-information)

**Important Information:**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/other-questions/subscriptions-and-billing#knowledge-base-token-quota-and-usage-management)

**Knowledge Base Token Quota and Usage Management**

1.  Files uploaded to the knowledge base only count toward your storage quota and won't incur any additional model usage charges.
    
2.  When you engage in conversations using the knowledge base, you will not consume any tokens. Rates depend on your chosen service tier (T1 or T2) and align with our standard conversation service pricing.
    
3.  For detailed information about quota for different subscription plans, please visit: [https://flowith.io/sub](https://flowith.io/sub)
    

**\*Clarification** :

We have noticed that some users are creating multiple Flowith accounts to circumvent limits and take advantage of our free tier to access our premium AI models. This abuse of our system negatively impacts the experience of other users.

If you have legitimate needs that exceed the standard usage limits, please reach out to our support team [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#32414742425d404672545e5d455b465a1c515d)
.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/other-questions/subscriptions-and-billing#refund-policy)

Refund Policy

*   Subscription fees are non-refundable
    
*   Refunds are available only if you meet the following conditions:
    
    *   Contact us within 48 hours after payment.
        
    *   You've made fewer than 200 credits throughout your account lifetime after subscription.
        
    

**Contact [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
:**

*   For any outstanding issues or special circumstances
    
*   For refund requests that meet our criteria
    
*   For technical difficulties with cancellation
    

**Contact Information:**

Email: [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b4c7c1c4c4dbc6c0f4d2d8dbc3ddc0dc9ad7db)

Discord: [https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD](https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD)

# Flowith へようこそ | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FzmBhbFHFJ6G9rBN4Fscb%2FOriginal5.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=395fc73b&sv=2)

flowith - AI for Deep Work

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso#flowith-toha)

**flowith とは？**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

flowith は、次世代の AI 生産性ツールです。従来のチャットベースの AI ツールとは異なり、flowith は二次元キャンバスを基にした対話方式を採用しています。これにより、単一のワークスペース内で複数のAI モデルと同時に対話することが可能となり、効率を大幅に向上させるコンテンツ生成や、創造プロセスにおけるフロー状態への没入を促進します。

flowith Oracle（フロウィズ オラクル）は、当社独自の次世代 AI エージェントシステムで、複数のステップを要する高度に複雑なタスクや要件を遂行するのに役立つよう設計されています。以下の機能をサポートしています：

*   自律的な計画立案
    
*   タスクの分解と完了
    
*   無制限のツール呼び出し
    
*   自己最適化と改善
    

**Oracle** は、AutoGPT などの従来のアーキテクチャと比較して、より成熟した安定したパフォーマンスを発揮します。さらに、flowithのキャンバスベースのインタラクションを活用することで、Oracle はより具体的な手順や包括的な情報をユーザーの皆様に分かりやすく提示することができます。

flowith **「Knowledge Garden」** ナレッジガーデンは、「AIとあなたの知識を自然に連携させる」 という中核理念に基づいて開発されました。自動的な知識整理、構造化された管理、そして創造的な協働を統合しています。文書、ノート、オンラインリソースを自動的にAIが理解できる最小知識単位（Seeds：ナレッジシード）に変換することができます。システムはAIによる知的分析を通じて、知識間の関連性を自動的に確立し、動的に成長する知識ネットワークを形成します。AIとの対話において、関連する知識が自動的に呼び出され、AIの応答の正確性と的確性が大幅に向上します。

製品情報: [flowith.io](https://flowith.io/)

公式ウェブサイト: [try.flowith.io](https://try.flowith.io/)

公式Twitter: @flowith\_ai

お問い合わせ先: [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
 Discord: [https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD](https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso#naze-flowith-wounoka)

なぜ flowith を使うのか？


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**より効率的なインタラクション**

従来のチャットUI の直線的な対話方式と比較して、flowith は二次元キャンバス形式のインタラクションを採用しています。これにより、以下のことが可能になります：

*   複数のスレッドで会話を展開
    
*   複数の分岐を作成
    
*   以下のようなシナリオに適しています：
    
    *   長文コンテンツの生成
        
    *   AI生成結果の比較
        
    *   プロンプトのデバッグ
        
    

これらの機能により、flowith はさまざまな複雑なタスクや創造的なプロセスに柔軟に対応できます。

**豊富なモデル選択**

単一の大規模言語モデルに限定されたやり取りとは異なり、当プラットフォームでは、ユーザーが選択できる多様なモデルを提供しています。これには以下が含まれます：

*   OpenAI: o1 Preview、GPT-4o、4o-mini、Claude 3.5 sonnet などのマルチモーダルモデル
    
*   Stable Diffusion や DALL·E 3 などの画像生成モデル
    

この多様性により、ユーザーは特定のニーズや用途に最適なモデルを選択することが可能になります。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FTtVJTQsDm4u5uvs2BZh2%2F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E4%25B8%25B0%25E5%25AF%258C%25E7%259A%2584%25E6%25A8%25A1%25E5%259E%258B%25E9%2580%2589%25E6%258B%25A9.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10d7fc3a&sv=2)

**リアルタイムコラボレーションと双方向機能**

flowith のキャンバスベースのインターフェースは、複数ユーザーによる共同作業に本質的に適しています。フローのリンクを同僚と共有することで、以下のことが可能になります：

*   生成された結果を直接閲覧する
    
*   あなたの創作プロセスに参加する
    
*   協力してコンテンツを生成し、デバッグする
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2F3qgCSWIVyADQFHDGk9ZE%2F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E6%259B%25B4%25E5%25A4%259A%25E7%259A%2584%25E4%25BA%2592%25E5%258A%25A8%25E5%25BD%25A2%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E5%2588%2586%25E4%25BA%25AB.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66ae3155&sv=2)

友達とリンクを共有

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2F7SZetZqxjiDUJYzX88hU%2F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E6%259B%25B4%25E5%25A4%259A%25E7%259A%2584%25E4%25BA%2592%25E5%258A%25A8%25E5%25BD%25A2%25E5%25BC%258F-%25E8%25AF%2584%25E8%25AE%25BA.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b202f684&sv=2)

Eコメント機能で対話的なディスカッションに参加

**効率的な問い合わせ方法**

Oracle モードでは、手動でのプロンプトエンジニアリングが不要になります。ユーザーは単に質問や要件を入力するだけで、Oracle が自律的に複雑なタスクの計画、分解、完了を行います。自動的に実行可能で編集可能な具体的なタスクステップを生成し提示するため、より実現可能で実用的な結果が得られます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Fd7ts3tVBaGoBgZE3dlAB%2F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E-%25E4%25BE%25BF%25E6%258D%25B7%25E7%259A%2584%25E6%258F%2590%25E9%2597%25AE%25E6%2596%25B9%25E5%25BC%258F.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d49b80b&sv=2)

オラクルモード：自動タスク分解

**ガイド付きフォローアップ質問**

従来の AI ツールは、ユーザーに必要な情報を尋ねることができず、曖昧で一般的な結果しか生成できないことがありました。一方、Oracle モードは積極的なアプローチを取ります。このモードでは、段階的な対話を行い、フォローアップ質問を通じて包括的かつ必要な詳細情報を収集します。この過程を経ることで、最終的にユーザーの具体的なニーズに合わせた高品質で深みのある最終出力を生成することができます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Fl81iVMczv8ILLFGxGDj5%2F%25E6%25AC%25A2%25E8%25BF%258E%2520-%2520%25E5%25BC%2595%25E5%25AF%25BC%25E5%25BC%258F%25E7%259A%2584%25E8%25BF%25BD%25E9%2597%25AE.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1214a1bb&sv=2)

フォローアップ質問で情報を充実

**無制限のツール連携**

Oracle モードは、外部ツール（プラグインと考えることができます）との連携をサポートしています。これには、Twitter やシャオホンシュー（小紅書）の検索、要約や推論、マインドマップの生成、PowerPoint プレゼンテーションの作成、ウェブページの生成などが含まれます。Oracle は、現在のサブタスクに応じて、ツールライブラリから最適なツールを自動的に選択し、必要に応じて呼び出します。

Oracle がサポートするツールの数は継続的に増加しており、そのフレームワークは無制限のツール連携を可能にしています。これにより、ユーザーは多様な機能を柔軟に活用することができます。

* * *

私たちは、人間同士のやりとりや協力と同様に、人間と AI の最適な対話方法も発散的、マルチスレッド的、そして協調的であるべきだと考えています。そのため、従来の会話型 GPT アシスタントとは全く異なる、革新的な AI 対話手法を開発しました。無限のキャンバス上で AI と自由に協働することで、アイデア創出の可能性を無限に広げると同時に、明確なプロセスを通じてアイデアを再利用可能なワークフローに変換することができます。

さあ、Flo を使って始めましょう！

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso#kuikkusutto)

**クイックスタート**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Flow モード ユーザーガイド](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/flow-mdo-mdo/flow-mdo-yzgaido)

[NextFlow モードの紹介](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/flow-mdo-mdo/flow-mdono)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Flow モードの紹介 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2F3GtBbyWKKz2HSlW0MPft%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE2.png&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99caed33&sv=2)

flow モードは、コンテンツクリエイター向けに特別に設計された次世代の AI 対話方式です。これは、flowith における標準的な対話方法として機能します。flowith は無限に広いキャンバスを活用しており、複数の AI アシスタントと同時にやり取りしながら、必要なコンテンツを生成することができます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2F3GtBbyWKKz2HSlW0MPft%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE2.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99caed33&sv=2)

**なぜ flow モードを使用するのか？**

単純な翻訳や基本的な質問応答だけで AI を利用する場合、従来のチャットモードで十分かもしれません。しかし、AI との多段階の会話や、以前の入力の修正、あるいは複数の AI アシスタントとの同時協働が必要な場合、flow モードは全く異なる創造的な体験を提供します。

flow モードを使用すると、より複雑なタスクや長期的なプロジェクトに対して、AI とのインタラクションを柔軟に管理できます。これにより、より効率的で生産的な作業環境を実現し、創造性を最大限に引き出すことができます。

**flow モードの利点：**

1.  **複数の AI インスタンスが並列スレッドで同時にコンテンツを生成できます。**
    
2.  **AI プロンプトを繰り返し修正し、複数回生成することができます。**
    
3.  **各ノードが他のノードのコンテンツを「参照」できるため、コンテンツの再利用が可能です。**
    
4.  **柔軟な情報の分岐と統合ができます。**
    
5.  **不要な情報をその場で削除できます。**
    
6.  **異なるモデルの生成結果を並行して簡単に比較できます。**
    
7.  ...
    

#### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/flow-mdo-mdo/flow-mdono#ysuksu)

ユースケース:

> flow モードでは、新しい会話を始めることなく、キャンバス内でモデルを簡単に切り替えることができます。例えば、「9.11と9.9のどちらが大きいか？」 という質問に対して、同じキャンバス上で複数の主要モデルの回答を比較できます。flowith の一般モードでは、ワンクリックでモデルを切り替えるだけでなく、各モデルのこの質問に対するパフォーマンスをキャンバス内に明確に表示します。これにより、結果をより効果的に比較することが可能になります。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FsAWfdIx0IQSPTVHDsT7N%2F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E4%25BB%258B%25E7%25BB%258D-%25E6%25A1%2588%25E4%25BE%258B-%25E4%25B8%2580%25E9%2594%25AE%25E5%2588%2587%25E6%258D%25A2%25E6%25A8%25A1%25E5%259E%258B.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28265d65&sv=2)

ワンクリックでモデル切り替え

> 1つのキャンバス内で、モデルの切り替えだけでなく、モード間を自由に切り替えることができます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Frj5DflZVr88MBoqvu4FM%2F%25E6%25B5%2581%25E5%25BC%258F%25E4%25BB%258B%25E7%25BB%258D-%25E6%2596%2587%25E6%259C%25ACmode%25E5%2588%2587%25E6%258D%25A2%25E5%259B%25BE%25E7%2589%2587mode.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d98131d4&sv=2)

「テキスト生成」 から 「画像生成」 へスムーズに移行

さらに、一般モードではテキストファイルや画像ファイルのアップロードにも対応しています。アップロードしたテキストファイルや画像ファイルに関連する質問をすることができます。

[高度な機能 — ノード参照](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/flow-mdo-mdo/na-ndo)

* * *

Flowの使用方法や機能に関する**追加情報**を、**継続的に更新**してまいります。

[PreviousFlowith へようこそ](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso)
[NextFlow モード ユーザーガイド](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/flow-mdo-mdo/flow-mdo-yzgaido)

Last updated 10 months ago

Was this helpful?

---

# Oracle モードはどのような問題解決に適していますか？ | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FLb1TccN0scGPrEBlzdlD%2FAmazing%2520Mockups.jpeg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50a313dc&sv=2)

Oracle モードは、複数のステップを要する複雑な課題や専門的な要件に対応するのに最適です。

Oracle モードでは、幅広い質問を提示すると、AI が一連の追加質問を通じて問題を絞り込み、具体化していきます：

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FyNbW5bohrczwWLOHQrIc%2FOracle-%25E4%25BB%2580%25E4%25B9%2588%25E6%25A0%25B7%25E7%259A%2584%25E9%2597%25AE%25E9%25A2%2598-1.%25E7%25BB%2586%25E5%258C%2596%25E9%2597%25AE%25E9%25A2%2598.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=561a9582&sv=2)

情報不足時の Oracle モードの追加質問機能

さらに、Oracle モードは、ユーザーの質問に基づいて独自に計画を立て、複雑なタスクを分解し、実行することができます。同時に、具体的で実行可能な実行プランを生成します。これにより、複数のステップを含む複雑な問題に特に適しています。

製品や現象について調査し、レポートを作成する必要がある場合、Oracle は優れた選択肢です。Oracleは様々なプラットフォームにわたってより包括的な検索を行うだけでなく、Webページや PowerPoint プレゼンテーションを生成する機能も活用します。これにより、必要な情報をより効果的に提示することができます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2F6qysYKWgJzr6O9cFQZy2%2FWebnew.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1e5c777&sv=2)

Oracle 生成の Web ページ

さらに、コミュニティ内の専門家が提供するテンプレートを検索、閲覧、または活用することができます。これらのリソースを使用することで、より簡単かつ明確にあなたの疑問を解決することができます。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FKmLmvdbROLspFLlX9Mf1%2FOracle-%25E4%25BB%2580%25E4%25B9%2588%25E6%25A0%25B7%25E7%259A%2584%25E9%2597%25AE%25E9%25A2%2598-3.%25E7%25A4%25BE%25E5%258C%25BA-edit.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=def7f672&sv=2)

コミュニティで利用可能な様々な専門的テンプレート

[PreviousOracle がサポートする現在の機能](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/oracle-gasaptosuruno)
[NextOracle モード ユーザーガイド](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/oracle-mdo-yzgaido)

Last updated 10 months ago

Was this helpful?
