# 高级玩法 — 节点引用 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/gao-ji-wan-fa-jie-dian-yin-yong#shen-me-shi-jie-dian)

什么是节点


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

节点是 Flowith 画布中的最小单位。每一个 AI 回复，每一个你的输入，都是一个节点。

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/gao-ji-wan-fa-jie-dian-yin-yong#ru-he-shi-yong-bian-liang-jie-dian)

如何使用变量节点


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

变量节点引用适用于频繁改变的内容（比如翻译中需要翻译的文本）。

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/gao-ji-wan-fa-jie-dian-yin-yong#chun-wen-ben)

纯文本

**插入节点**

1.  点击左上角工具栏里 「变量节点」 按钮并拖拽到画布中
    
2.  修改节点的名字
    
3.  输入内容
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FPgiTvKeflNEubPlaMMIK%252F%25E6%258F%2592%25E5%2585%25A5%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7541e82-a87c-41ec-9930-1372e09fb397&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e2766d0&sv=2)

在画布中插入一个节点

**引用节点**

1.  将光标移动到需要插入处
    
2.  点击画布下方的圆形按钮
    
3.  选择 「引用其他节点内容」
    
4.  点击你所要引用的节点
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FfdpEA9t9iwJYkV7hqWH5%252F%25E5%25BC%2595%25E7%2594%25A8%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5dca7966-d9f9-40d3-9de9-b28f5d6f9e8a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=559c56c&sv=2)

当画布变暗时就可以选择要引用的节点

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/gao-ji-wan-fa-jie-dian-yin-yong#shang-chuan-wen-ben-wen-jian-huo-tu-pian)

上传文本文件或图片

**上传文本文件**

1.  将光标移动到需要插入处
    
2.  点击画布下方的圆形按钮
    
3.  选择 「上传文本文件进行提问」
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FgeFu56O2i0GvZVg4UZzM%252F%25E4%25B8%258A%25E4%25BC%25A0%25E6%2596%2587%25E6%259C%25AC%25E6%2596%2587%25E4%25BB%25B6.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D811eaf6d-078b-4142-9a42-3387275b0979&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=618ea858&sv=2)

文本文件作为 「插入节点」 展现在画布中

**上传图片文件**

1.  将光标移动到需要插入处
    
2.  点击画布下方的圆形按钮
    
3.  选择 「上传图片进行提问」
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FJ8Ix2SlVtihhmpm3G7EA%252F%25E4%25B8%258A%25E4%25BC%25A0%25E5%259B%25BE%25E7%2589%2587.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2c7b982-c8b1-4c5e-a63a-8246cb623309&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a435c15&sv=2)

图片作为 「插入节点」 展现在画布中

# 知识花园功能简介 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FUopBhOuVucfMLtuovA6j%252F1280X1280.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7e4dc85-0590-4245-ada2-b4308f36ef2c&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16bcc41a&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-gong-neng-jian-jie#wei-shen-me-yao-shi-yong-flowith-jin-xing-zhi-shi-guan-li)

为什么要使用 flowith 进行知识管理


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FUopBhOuVucfMLtuovA6j%252F1280X1280.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7e4dc85-0590-4245-ada2-b4308f36ef2c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16bcc41a&sv=2)

不管你是内容创作者、学生、设计师、程序员、管理者还是任何形式的知识工作者，哪怕你已经对各类 AI 工具的使用了如指掌，你一定还是对我提到的这些痛点深有同感：

1.  **信息离散无序**：笔记、文档分散在各个软件、文件夹、浏览器标签，知识无法形成体系化的沉淀，难以快速找到需要的信息；每次启动工作时，你面对的都是一个个空白页面，然后需要在无数文件、软件与页面间四处搜索和拷贝信息，重头开始或撰写或编撰成冗长的 prompt 喂给 AI。
    
2.  **协作隔离低效**：你和你的团队成员的知识无法共享，每次都要寻找一个数个月甚至数年前的文档上的某段信息，导致沟通成本高昂、产出质量参差不齐。
    
3.  **AI 生成内容没有针对性**：大语言模型过于通用，AI 缺乏个人知识和专业领域的理解，导致难以根据个人背景产生符合要求的内容并且容易产生"幻觉"给出错误信息，无法确保回答的一致性。
    

人们被迫屈从于格式和工具的桎梏，而非集中精力于知识本身的逻辑结构和创新表达，这在今天的 Generative AI 时代，显得格外落伍，犹如用打孔纸带来建造火箭。

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-gong-neng-jian-jie#ai-shi-dai-de-zhi-shi-guan-li-yu-chuang-zuo-shen-me-shi-flowith-zhi-shi-guan-li-mo-kuai)

**AI 时代的知识管理与创作——**什么是 flowith 知识管理模块？


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

联通 AI 时代的知识管理和创作，flowith 2.0 推出了全新的 「Knowledge Garden」 知识花园，它是一个基于 AI Agent 的新一代知识管理系统，帮助你大幅提高 AI 创作效果与效率的同时进行自动化的个人知识管理：

*   **快速创建个人知识库**：无需从头开始，只要导入已有的资料和文件，flowith AI 就会借助 Seed 系统将其自动分解为知识的最小单元进行自动化知识管理、快速搭建你的 AI 知识库。
    
*   **自动化匹配和生成：**在你使用 AI 进行特定任务时，flowith 会自动匹配你选择的知识库下有价值的信息，这让 flowith 知识库成为一个真正智能、有生命力的第二大脑系统，帮助你更自然地管理和运用知识。
    
*   **联通知识管理和内容生成：**你的内容会被自动建立关联，形成一个有机且智能的知识网络，确保回答的准确性并有效避免“幻觉”现象，显著提升生成质量。
    
*   **显著降低使用门槛：**专注在个人知识库的搭建，而非复杂的提示词工程上，即可与 AI 进行自然的对话，使用和共享社区知识库，帮助你大幅节省工作成本或是让你的知识盈利。
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FgCaRsPaS3EQnyB6PT6y4%252F%25E7%2583%25AD%25E5%258A%259B%25E5%259B%25BE.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ecf71dc-94fe-45a5-949d-b1def9f24025&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c42b6bcf&sv=2)

Knowledge Garden 功能将 LLM 的技术特性和人类卡片知识管理思维相结合，让 AI 更好的读懂、利用人类的私有化知识，帮助人们更有针对性、更高质量的生成内容。同时 Knowledge Garden 里的信息对人类来说，也可以用作更高效的知识管理。

总而言之，如果你的知识类型学习和工作是一场游戏，flowith 就为你打造了一个 「外挂」 级的 AI 知识管理系统，让你获得当前市面上所有产品中所能得到最高质量的 AI 生成效果。

[PreviousPrompt Engineering 基础](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/prompt-engineering-ji-chu)
[Next知识花园案例](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-an-li)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

# 关于 Oracle 模式 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FdhFjmMPclhNzJp7dhZ1c%252F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02f9f800-a62e-4b49-9d4b-20327cfdece0&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c56180c&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/guan-yu-oracle-mo-shi#shen-me-shi-oracle)

什么是 Oracle


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

这是由 flowith 团队开发的最先进的、以通用人工智能（pre-AGI）为目标设计的的智能体系统，专为处理多步骤、复杂、需要使用更多工具的任务而设计。

它的功能包括自主规划任务、任务分解、无限制工具使用和自我优化。Oracle 的外部能力会不断更新和升级。使其随着时间的推移变得越来越强。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FCIDy6htAMfmo3KDXw8ZE%252FAmazing%2520Mockups.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5dd6082-4b4d-4f4a-978a-c5fc8a9bc77e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ac5926a&sv=2)

Oracle Recipe and Nodes

**换句话说，Oracle is a data-level**（数据层级别的、而不具备物理介质或和现实世界交互的）generalized (可以完成通用的任务、而非只有他被训练、或定义过的任务) **Agent**（不只是 LLM，可以调用工具、管理记忆、多 LLM 协作） that can complete complex tasks （不只是完成简单的问题或命令）and adapt to new situations（在新的环境或任务下可以自我学习和处理）.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/guan-yu-oracle-mo-shi#he-xin-gai-nian)

核心概念


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Recipe 工作流**

Recipe 一词原意是指配方、烹饪方法。对于 Oracle 来说，Recipe 是指 AI 在去完成用户任务时，去执行的一套系统性工作流。当每次用户输入完需求或指令，Oracle 都会整体的指令进行拆解，根据它自身的能力和可调用的工具，把整体任务拆成一步一步自任务，然后再交给任务分配器去一步步执行。

在每次 Oracle 设计完一整套 Recipe 后，它都会与用户确认，随后才开始执行，用户在确认过程中可以直接修改 Recipe 里的具体执行步骤，包括调整顺序、删除、修改文字和增加新的步骤。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FEFYpRO4ie9zxqLfGqxad%252F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deef0fe07-00ce-40fe-af4d-b8d5209b5823&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7db10423&sv=2)

A Recipe Generated by Oracle

**Dispatcher 任务分配器**

任务分配器是指每一条 Oracle 生成的自任务在被执行时，会有一个分配任务的 Agent 把子任务进行分配和落地执行，它会从 Oracle 支持的工具库里找到最合适的工具，然后把子任务进行执行和完成。

比如，当子任务是 「搜索 flowith 在社交媒体上的用户评价」 ，任务分配器会调用 「Twitter 搜索工具」 、 「Reddit 搜索工具」 、「谷歌搜索工具」 进行对 flowith 用户评价的搜索。

你可以在 Oracle 对话发起页面中查看目前 Oracle 所支持的工具，这个列表会实时更新，我们也将持续把最有用的工具添加到 Oracle 所支持的工具库中。

[Oracle 目前所支持的能力](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mu-qian-suo-zhi-chi-de-neng-li)

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FTMrTvG0vDQ7aeyQ9mim6%252F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a3791e7-d36f-48f0-bc6c-e65c5203315f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3213cf5b&sv=2)

Tools supported by Oracle

**Memory 记忆和上下文管理**

Oracle 是为复杂工作而生，因此对于步骤较多的工作，会产生大量的上下文，如果我们将所有上文内容交给 LLM，则将影响它的工作表现。

因此 Oracle 在任务分配、执行的过程中，会智能的选择性使用上文信息，比如当 Oracle 执行到第 10 步时，它的记忆管理器会判断以上哪些步骤的信息是有必要的，并将必要的信息放入当前步骤的上文。因此，你无需担心上文过长的问题。

**自我迭代和更新 Recipe**

在每一步执行完后，Oracle 都会根据每一步骤的执行结果，对整个 Recipe 进行必要的更新，比如当它没有搜到需要的信息，它会给接下来的步骤中加入更多的搜索，以便它可以顺利完成任务。

当 Oracle 询问是否满意结果时，如果用户表示不满意，它也将生成更多的步骤，尝试为用户提供想要的结果。

[Previous知识花园变现指南](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan)
[NextOracle 目前所支持的能力](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mu-qian-suo-zhi-chi-de-neng-li)

Last updated 10 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Oracle 模式高级玩法 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FdhFjmMPclhNzJp7dhZ1c%252F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D02f9f800-a62e-4b49-9d4b-20327cfdece0&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c56180c&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-gao-ji-wan-fa#ru-he-xiu-gai-recipe)

如何修改 Recipe


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   当一条 recipe 太长时，可以在触控板上滑动来读取后面的内容
    
*   需要删除某条 recipe 时，勾选该条后方的 「垃圾桶」 图标
    
*   点击页面左下角的 「＋」 ，即可添加一条新的步骤
    
*   点击某条前方的 「拖拽」 符号并拖拽，即可把该条放在你想要的位置
    
*   调整完全部 recipe 后，点击 「Confirm & Run」 ，即可运行
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FSN0p5uYzykl7QJ0ZpFut%252F%25E4%25BF%25AE%25E6%2594%25B9recipe.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7d2928a-d308-4957-9684-f1fa38bf8f44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eeec7f93&sv=2)

修改 recipe

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-gao-ji-wan-fa#ru-he-jiang-zi-ji-zhi-ding-de-recipe-fen-xiang-dao-she-qu)

如何将自己制定的 Recipe 分享到社区


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

你可以将你你反复打磨的 recipe 分享到社区，让大家一起来体验你的智慧成果。

1.  点击 「Share」
    
2.  点击 「Publish to Community」
    
3.  填写必要信息并发布！
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FXJcXJIUwNcrva5MROirO%252F%25E5%2588%2586%25E4%25BA%25ABrecipe.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e9cd98e-22c7-45d5-8616-f90f4191eff1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c90255b&sv=2)

详细填写模板信息

[PreviousOracle 模式使用指南](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan)

# 如何反馈问题 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

如果您在使用过程中遇到任何问题或者有任何建议，欢迎联系我们。

**通过邮箱**

官方邮箱：[\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

**通过产品页面**

1.  点击产品页面 「[flowith.io](https://flowith.io/)
    」 的左下角 「订阅与设置」
    
2.  点击 「订阅与设置」 中的 「反馈联系」
    
3.  加入discord
    

[Previous关于订阅](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue)
[Next信息搜集 + 整理大师](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/ying-yong-an-li/xin-xi-sou-ji-+-zheng-li-da-shi)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

# 关于订阅 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue#ding-yue-fang-an)

订阅方案


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

我们提供了极具性价比的订阅方案，提供 OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、DeepSeek、Meta 等公司的顶尖 AI 模型支持。除此之外，我们也接入了支持生成图片和视频的顶尖模型。

详情请见：[https://flowith.io/sub](https://flowith.io/sub)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue#chao-ji-mo-xing-oracle)

超级模型—— Oracle


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

在 Oracle 模式中，每一步都会消耗一个 T-1 配额。例如，一个需要六个步骤的任务将使用 6 个 T-1 额度。

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue#zhi-shi-ku)

知识库


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **文件存储计费机制**
    

文件上传至知识库时，仅计入知识库存储空间配额，不产生额外的模型调用费用。

1.  **对话服务计费规则**
    

当通过知识库发起对话时，系统将根据所选用模型的服务层级（T1级别、T2级别）进行模型调用次数的计量计费，计费标准与基础对话服务保持一致。

1.  **存储配额管理**
    

关于知识库存储配额的具体限制及管理规范，请参阅：[https://flowith.io/sub](https://flowith.io/sub)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

注意事项：


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**政策说明：**

我们发现部分用户通过批量注册大量 Flowith 账号，滥用免费额度调用我们成本高昂的 AI 模型，这种行为严重影响了其他用户的正常使用体验。

若您遇到特殊情况达到调用上限，请联系我们。

联系方式：

邮箱：[\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

Discord：[https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD](https://discord.com/invite/g95B77xbpD)

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/guan-yu-ding-yue#tui-kuan-zheng-ce)

退款政策

*   订阅费用通常不可退款
    
*   仅在同时满足以下情况可申请退款：
    
    *   在支付成功后48小时内联系我们
        
    *   订阅后账户累计使用Credits少于200
        
    

如遇以下情况，请联系 [\[email protected\]](https://doc.flowith.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

*   任何未尽事宜或特殊情况
    
*   对于符合退款条件的申请
    
*   关于取消订阅的技术问题咨询
    

[PreviousOracle 模式高级玩法](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-gao-ji-wan-fa)
[Next如何反馈问题](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/qi-ta-wen-ti/ru-he-fan-kui-wen-ti)

# 知识花园变现指南 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

AI 时代的知识付费生态将迎来全新的范式转变，传统基于图文和视频的知识创作将慢慢被淘汰，基于 AI 的知识创作和分发将成为未来的主流。flowith 作为当前海内外市场上用户量最大的画布式 AI 生成工具于 2025 年推出了 「知识市场 Knowledge Marketbase」 ——我们希望 flowith 能成为 AI 时代知识创造者的 「OnlyFans」 ，帮助创作者收获更多的收益和曝光，给使用者提供更多价值。

目前，已经有我们合作的知识博主在内测期间**通过发布其原创的财富管理知识库，在短短两周内获得了超过 2000 位用户的测试，并创造了超过 2 万元的收入。**

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#shen-me-shi-flowith-zhi-shi-shi-chang)

什么是 flowith 知识市场


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FIKBz2MIWVN8wPnQdsQ4O%252F%25E7%259F%25A5%25E8%25AF%2586%25E5%25B8%2582%25E5%259C%25BA.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc79b71c9-5ed9-4215-979a-ea1b0ab2ae1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9845652&sv=2)

尽管大语言模型在大规模通用语料上已学到大量知识，但其参数记忆有限且难以及时获取最新、最具体、私有化的专业信息。通过在使用中引入外部知识库，可动态补充和检索所需内容，减少模型幻觉，提升准确度及可控性，显著增强 LLM 的生成质量与应用价值。联通 AI 时代的知识管理和创作，flowith 通过自研的 agenic knowledge management 框架可以将用户上传的信息和文件高效拆分为 knowledge seed，并使用自动化的知识管理进行结构化的存储和整理。在用户后续使用 AI 时可以自动匹配相关的知识种子，从而大幅度提高 AI 的回复质量、针对性、有效性。

简而言之，你可以将 flowith 知识库理解为大语言模型的 「知识外挂」 ，通过引入这些 「外挂」 ，大模型可以拥有你和团队的独家信息，获得当前市面上所有 AI 生成类产品中所能得到最高质量的生成和创作效果。而知识市场就是这些知识库的市集，允许用户分享免费的知识库或使用知识库进行内容变现。

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#ru-he-chuang-jian-yi-ge-hao-de-zhi-shi-ku)

如何创建一个好的知识库


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

像几乎任何领域的内容创作一样，要在 flowith 上创建一个可以给你的用户提供价值并为你自己带来收益的知识库有两种方法：

1.  **原创（Creation）**：如果你已经是一位知识和内容创作者或者博主，太好了！除了传统基于图片、文字、视频的内容分发，flowith 为你提供了一条额外通过内容变现的方式：AI。你只需要将自己的原创内容按照不同方式导入 flowith 就可以进行分享和上架。
    
2.  **策展（Curation）：**在这个信息繁杂丰富的时代，互联网已经为每个人提供了足够多的素材和优质内容，难点并不在于缺乏信息，而在于筛选和整理其中有洞见和价值的那些。你可以将互联网上的优质内容按照特定主题进行整理和收集并上传到 flowith 知识库当中，就可以开始使用内容变现了。
    

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#yuan-wen-jian-shang-chuan-zhi-nan)

源文件上传指南


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252Fory1suXUnPBj75mjprxi%252Fzhong%25201.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D049e660f-fee5-42d4-9991-ce80c2d1505b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8156128b&sv=2)

*   **长度要求：**
    
    *   内容长度灵活，可处理包含相关关键词的任意文本
        
    *   不支持文本摘要生成功能
        
    *   超过1,000字符的源文本将自动分段处理
        
    
*   **文件格式规范：**
    
    *   无特定格式限制，但不支持PDF图像识别
        
    *   图片需单独上传，嵌入长文本中的图片将被忽略
        
    *   不支持代码的读取和处理
        
    
*   **支持的内容类型：**
    
    *   支持单独的图片上传
        
    *   完全支持基于文本的内容
        
    *   长篇内容需要分段处理
        
    

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#zai-zhi-shi-shi-chang-fa-bu-he-ying-xiao-ni-de-zhi-shi-ku)

在知识市场发布和营销你的知识库


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FHdxB88TKt77RojJ57AeQ%252F%25E7%259F%25A5%25E8%25AF%2586%25E5%25B8%2582%25E5%259C%25BA2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcaaff5d8-6621-47fa-a8fb-70add644dbe8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea22b61a&sv=2)

创建一个好的知识库只是第一步：Knowledge Market 是用户进行浏览和购买知识库的平台，flowith 的大量的社区用户在此寻觅适合自己、能够解决自己问题的知识库，并为此付费。明晰且具有吸引力的名字和描述可以帮助你的知识库脱颖而出，获得更多用户的青睐——自然帮助你获取更多潜在收益。

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#zhi-shi-ku-miao-shu-zen-me-xie)

知识库描述怎么写

#### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#yi-qi-yi-ge-hao-ming-zi)

一、起一个好名字

*   单一信源知识库
    

如果是单一信源的知识库，我们建议直接使用信息源的名字：如孙子兵法

*   合集、专栏、复合型知识库
    

如果你的知识库是一个复合型的知识库，可以选择一个能清晰简洁地描述整体主题的标题。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FXeq5kmz3zMBxMHHlVaHJ%252Fzhong%25202.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c0fa4bf-1437-41e0-b10b-3f27cd8dc32b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b6543ea&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/zhi-shi-hua-yuan-bian-xian-zhi-nan#er-zhuan-xie-hao-de-miao-shu)

二、撰写好的描述

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FKSLivUkeEVFPmfIRdWnq%252Fzhong%25203.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66a9bc51-9dc6-4f0a-ad4e-d3945b412afb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcb19f8&sv=2)

好的知识库描述是你的门面，能让用户快速理解其价值和用途。根据经验，我们建议你从以下四个方面进行说明：

1.  **信息来源：**明确说明知识内容的来源渠道、标注信息的时效性和更新频率、注明作者或维护团队的背景
    
2.  **知识库特点：**概述知识库的主要内容范围、说明知识组织的方式和结构、突出知识库的独特优势或特色
    
3.  **目标用户：**明确定义适用的用户群体、描述用户可能的使用场景
    
4.  **价值主张：**指出这个知识库能解决什么具体问题、说明用户可以获得什么收益、描述预期达到的学习或应用效果
    

Copy

    例如:
    这是一个面向前端开发者的 React 最佳实践知识库。内容来自我们团队3年的项目实践总结，每月更新。
    通过系统化的组件开发指南和性能优化建议，帮助开发者提升代码质量，加快项目开发效率。

记住：描述要简洁清晰，让用户在短时间内就能判断这个知识库是否适合自己。同时要确保描述的真实性，不要过度承诺。

[Previous如何建立和使用知识库](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/knowledge-garden/ru-he-jian-li-he-shi-yong-zhi-shi-ku)
[Next关于 Oracle 模式](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/guan-yu-oracle-mo-shi)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

# 流式聊天使用指南 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic-2v.gitbook.com%2F_next%2Fstatic%2Fmedia%2Fdefault-page-cover.a2ccd7e9.svg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=899888f5&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#kai-shi-chuang-jian)

开始创建


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

点击 「新对话」 后：

1.  在对话框中输入问题，注意要保持 Oracle 模式关闭
    
2.  如果需要自定义模型，可在左下方选择模型
    
3.  点击 Start 按钮
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FxSwA7sX4kAhRjsu0fFBk%252F9.11%25E5%2592%258C9.9%25E5%2593%25AA%25E4%25B8%25AA%25E5%25A4%25A7.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff9f545b-5854-4259-a96e-7ccbfe6f177b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96a8e3b9&sv=2)

开启新对话

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#dui-ai-gei-chu-de-hui-da-ji-xu-zhui-wen)

对 AI 给出的回答继续追问


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  点击想追问的节点
    
2.  在对话框中输入你想提问的问题
    
3.  按下 Enter 键
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FpT2fTgC3wqaSQi2tK8Dw%252F%25E8%25BF%25BD%25E9%2597%25AE.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb79805c-94e5-4e67-ae51-8bbbec578c63&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4451366d&sv=2)

对 AI 的回答可以进行进一步追问

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#chong-xin-sheng-cheng-te-ding-jie-dian-zhong-de-nei-rong)

重新生成特定节点中的内容


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

对节点中的内容不满意时，点击重新运行节点，即可一键生成新的内容

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FAdJJyqAxtw8L4yikDYfh%252F%25E9%2587%258D%25E6%2596%25B0%25E8%25BF%2590%25E8%25A1%258C.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50892876-7f70-4291-9282-c79284304db1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd696a8&sv=2)

一键重新运行该节点

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#zhan-kai-jie-dian-zhong-de-nei-rong)

展开节点中的内容


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如果节点中的内容过多不便于展示，

1.  选中节点
    
2.  点击 「展开节点」 即可
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FIlNt5ZVlA0rplwSCZ8js%252F%25E5%25B1%2595%25E5%25BC%2580.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1c3726b-fa8d-4cc0-bbc4-53f388144a1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90ee78fe&sv=2)

展开节点查看完整内容

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#fu-zhi-jie-dian-zhong-de-jie-guo)

复制节点中的结果


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  选中节点
    
2.  点击 「复制节点」
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252F3DfE0GifEEk85bd27k9o%252F%25E5%25A4%258D%25E5%2588%25B6%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8033ff2-713a-441f-b320-b182f264259a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61cc96a9&sv=2)

对生成的内容一键复制

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#shan-chu-jie-dian)

删除节点


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**删除单个节点**

1.  选中节点
    
2.  点击 「删除节点」
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FxCUkZEktplqP1p04rniv%252F%25E5%2588%25A0%25E9%2599%25A4%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73e02308-e41e-4053-9a73-34737ce2c8cb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aa8a9df1&sv=2)

一键删除节点

**删除多个节点**

1.  按住 「shift」 键，依次点击想要删除的多个节点
    
2.  按下 「backspace」 键
    
3.  确认删除
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FuY4dqDZEMpTxP35JUbwv%252F%25E5%2588%25A0%25E9%2599%25A4%25E5%25A4%259A%25E4%25B8%25AA%25E8%258A%2582%25E7%2582%25B9.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D168bf960-cece-4c6f-8876-d386e9857ce8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8e78002&sv=2)

需要长按 「shift」 键

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#fen-xiang-wo-de-flow-gei-peng-you)

分享我的 flow 给朋友


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  点击页面左上角的 Share
    
2.  选择权限 「可查看」
    
3.  复制链接并分享
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252Fob84pkgUw3g2EqrqCAjI%252F%25E5%2588%2586%25E4%25BA%25AB%25E7%25BB%2599%25E6%259C%258B%25E5%258F%258B.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D595a185e-253c-4895-b4bd-adc73dd27a87&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1d1ac54&sv=2)

邀请朋友欣赏你的创意

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/flowith-normal/liu-shi-liao-tian-shi-yong-zhi-nan#yao-qing-peng-you-gong-tong-chuang-zuo)

邀请朋友共同创作


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  点击页面左上角的 Share
    
2.  选择权限 「可编辑」
    
3.  复制链接并分享
    
4.  使用评论功能在画布中进行交流
    
    1.  点击页面左上角 「插入评论」
        
    2.  点击你想要的评论的节点
        
    3.  再次点击页面左上角的 「插入评论」 退出
        
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FcEBs1PXmi8j89x0hEe74%252F%25E5%2585%25B1%25E5%2588%259B1.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df282a7c7-1843-41d8-9dba-62afc6f6caa7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a00df74&sv=2)

开启编辑权限并分享

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252F3aMhNnC2z3dvaGmAzxhH%252F%25E6%258F%2592%25E5%2585%25A5%25E8%25AF%2584%25E8%25AE%25BA.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76d0bb0b-db35-49fb-aaa1-24d90107de34&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddbc8a2&sv=2)

点击节点并评论

# Oracle 模式使用指南 | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FIoGBv6KmDuBGVIrYtsfM%252F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc51d1b64-dc29-4d04-a197-e95cb7aa7124&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bbf8cc9c&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan#kai-shi)

开始


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  在对话框中输入问题
    
2.  打开 Oracle 模式
    
3.  点击 Start
    
4.  查看 planner 并点击 「Confirm & Run」 执行
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FjlrwtzJoOQ94RMVOrbNx%252FOracle%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%25A7%258B%25E5%2588%259B%25E5%25BB%25BA.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ca1ed03-f72f-4fad-9af8-8c6f8d0c01fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b48726af&sv=2)

「ORACLE MODE」 要保持打开

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan#cha-kan-recipe-de-zhi-xing-jin-du)

查看 Recipe 的执行进度


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  选中一个节点
    
2.  将光标滑动到页面下方输入框
    
3.  查看 Recipe 的执行进度
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252F7YffjwPs8fosNtW18bRB%252F%25E6%259F%25A5%25E7%259C%258BPlanner.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87e398d3-6840-49df-ac00-e8c7230176b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81db7773&sv=2)

每一条步骤前的圆圈表明该条步骤的状态

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan#chong-fu-zhi-xing-shang-yi-ge-recipe)

重复执行上一个 Recipe


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  点击你想查看的 recipe 的任意一个节点
    
2.  将光标移动到对话框上，recipe 会自动弹出
    
3.  点击 「Re-run」，会弹出确认页面
    
4.  点击 「Confirm & Run」
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FwNqNDtPaqKKQYZReRhbd%252F%25E9%2587%258D%25E5%25A4%258D%25E6%2589%25A7%25E8%25A1%258C.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21cb2613-04e5-44f4-adf5-e0e952c7e4ec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=69a04a9b&sv=2)

重复执行上一个 recipe

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan#ru-he-zai-tong-yi-ge-hua-bu-zhong-kai-qi-xin-fen-zhi)

如何在同一个画布中开启新分支


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

点击 「New Branch」 后，在页面下方的对话框中输入新问题即可开启新分支。

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FnDA7SRBSXcnh0vf6AJrM%252F%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%2590%25AF%25E6%2596%25B0%25E5%2588%2586%25E6%2594%25AF.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3ef4f015-7f8d-4c63-b532-ef4f59fd5dab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c261fec3&sv=2)

一个画布中可以开启多个分支

[](https://doc.flowith.io/cn/oracle-mode-zhi-neng-ti-mo-shi/oracle-mo-shi-shi-yong-zhi-nan#ru-he-shi-yong-recipe-mu-ban)

如何使用 Recipe 模板


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  在 「发现」 搜索想要的模板关键字
    
2.  点击 「Use this recipe」 查看详情
    
3.  点击 「Confirm & Run」 即可使用模板
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3657150132-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAVkWkYQheefIjsWOM7id%252Fuploads%252FaB5P8Xlsn6N0QuSHrv7v%252F%25E4%25BD%25BF%25E7%2594%25A8%25E6%25A8%25A1%25E6%259D%25BF.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd38b91a9-47ec-4f1f-87d0-4c22a63739f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a768af2e&sv=2)

社区中有专业的模板可供选择

# Canvas Navigation in Agent Mode | Flowith Official Document

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#canvas-execution-prompt-to-plan)

Canvas Execution: Prompt to Plan


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-1.-prompt-parsing-and-seed-discovery)

1\. Prompt Parsing and Seed Discovery

*   **Trigger:** User enters a prompt and activates Neo in Agent Mode.
    
*   **Process:** Neo analyzes the prompt for **key terms**, including:
    
    *   Named entities (e.g., **“May 2025 Sales Report”**, **“Q2 Consumer Behavior Summary”**, **“Chimera GPU Whitepaper”**)
        
    *   Goal-based language (e.g., “summarize”, “generate”, “compare”)
        
    

> This parsing is automatic. No special formatting is needed by the user — Neo extracts intent and targets naturally from conversational input.

*   **Knowledgebase Usage (if enabled):** Neo queries the **Knowledge Base** for any contextually matching documents. These documents are converted into “**seeds**” — key fragments of relevant data — which are used to **grow a context-aware Recipe**.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252F49KhLtryS4WaaDR70oTR%252FKowledge_Base_Load.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ed86a2f-fb32-46e6-9fc6-77de7fb919ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a2d677c&sv=2)

Agent Neo Scanning the enabled Knowledge Base

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-2.-knowledge-garden-and-recipe-generation)

2\. Knowledge Garden and Recipe Generation

*   **Concept:** Neo builds a **Recipe**, a living execution plan made up of evolving subtasks.
    
*   **With Knowledge Base Enabled:**
    
    *   Extracted seeds are used to **enrich** the Recipe with domain-specific context.
        
    *   Seeds are re-quoted inside the canvas so you can trace what context was used.
        
    
*   **Without Knowledge Base:**
    
    *   Neo builds a base-level Recipe using model knowledge, tools, and live search.
        
    
*   **Additional Controls:**
    
    *   You can **pause** an active Recipe at any time to temporarily halt execution.
        
    *   You can also **duplicate** a Recipe to fork it into a new session for experimentation or comparison.
        
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-3.-task-planning-and-tool-allocation)

3\. Task Planning and Tool Allocation

Once the Recipe is seeded:

*   **Neo activates the Dispatcher.** This allocator breaks down the Recipe into actionable subtasks and selects tools for each step.
    
*   **Toolset Sampling:** Based on your goal, Neo dynamically selects from tools such as:
    
    *   Web Search
        
    *   Code Generator
        
    *   File Uploader
        
    *   Chart Interpreter
        
    *   Terminal (if enabled)
        
    
*   **Live Plan Rendering:** The Recipe and subtasks are visualized directly in the canvas. Each task node can be expanded to see:
    
    *   Chosen Tool
        
    *   Reasoning
        
    *   Output
        
    *   Follow-up tasks (auto-generated)
        
    

> If a task fails, Neo re-routes. It will adapt the Recipe and try alternative tools or updated phrasing — even mid-plan. The remaining steps to complete the task is estimated by Neo and displayed at the bottom of the recipe list

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FbdDreUnNJd7M1Ak6B8ME%252FRecipe_Execution.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93d323cd-35cb-456c-a38d-3699adbe4058&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b36cca9b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-4.-execution-begins)

4\. Execution Begins

After the plan is finalized, the **Start** button launches execution.

*   You can pause, stop, or adjust task inputs live.
    

> Neo continues refining the Recipe in real time, responding to results, user edits, and discovered context. This dynamic execution lets Neo outperform static agents that cannot re-plan.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#common-node-types-in-neos-canvas)

Common Node Types in Neo's Canvas


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As Neo executes a task, it dynamically generates **node blocks** inside the canvas. Each node represents a specific action or tool usage within the current Recipe. Understanding these common node types helps you trace Neo’s reasoning and interact more effectively with ongoing or completed plans.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-1.-gen-document-node)

1\. Gen Document Node

**Purpose:** Neo uses this node to draft written plans such as **roadmaps**, **task briefs**, and **multi-step strategies** based on the current Recipe context.

*   **Features:**
    
    *   Click the **down arrow** icon to expand or collapse the full document view (appears on the right side of the screen).
        
    *   Documents are version-aware and update based on upstream changes in the Recipe.
        
    

> Tip: Review the Documents to provide more concise follow-ups with neo about edits. You can also Right Click this node to directly add the contents to your Knowledge Base

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FM9k8D68wd2tdjoljwinJ%252FGen_Document.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43e18fc6-cb1f-4b4b-920d-dd5aab6553b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c25e367&sv=2)

Click the Down Arrow to expand contents on the right of screen

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-2.-online-search-node)

2\. Online Search Node

**Purpose:** Triggers a deep search across multiple platforms to gather external data necessary for informed task planning.

*   **Features:**
    
    *   Displays links and excerpts from search results.
        
    *   Includes a **source toggle** to reveal or hide exact URLs and timestamps.
        
    *   Neo may create multiple Online Search nodes per task if additional data is required.
        
    

> Example: Searching for “Chimera GPU specs” results in this node, which then influences downstream coding or writing steps.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FR9A2wgV3bpLI62d0h8Zb%252FSearch_Tool_Node.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90a30935-02f7-4efc-bfc0-9c777a82dfa6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=247f4be&sv=2)

Click the Toggle Button below the Node to view sources

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-3.-gen-webpage-node)

3\. Gen Webpage Node

**Purpose:** This is Neo’s **code generation node**, typically used for writing websites, frontends, scripts, or downloadable source files. You can click the Down Arrow icon to review the code

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fc4F4IXPlcCk5OWmSjpGk%252Fgen_webpage.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db54e3493-d490-49ed-ad46-0557b82b5322&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5a0f70a3&sv=2)

Click the Toggle Button to review Source Code similar to Gen Document Node

**Features:**

*   Refine with Neo: Prompt Neo to edit anything rendered inside the node
    
*   Edit in Fullscreen: Opens an inline fullscreen editor
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252F4M0ARJlBoFPKQ3AvunYr%252Fedit_webpage.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c3d807d-56e7-482e-8f92-ee2c695a1c5a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50d21bfc&sv=2)

Easily Reposition and Edit Elements

*   Open in New Tab: Launches the code output in a sandboxed preview
    
*   Download: Saves the raw code as a ZIP file
    

> This node is used extensively for technical recipes involving HTML, JS, CSS, Markdown, or static site builds.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-4.-all-task-coimplete-node)

4\. All Task Coimplete Node

**Purpose:** Signals that Neo has finished executing all Recipe steps.

*   **Features:**
    
    *   Shows a **completion banner** inside the canvas.
        
    *   Contains a **follow-up input dialog** so you can extend or refine the task without resetting the entire canvas.
        
    

> You can treat this as a checkpoint — review the output, save results, or continue iterating.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-5.-ask-user-more-node)

5\. Ask User More Node

**Purpose:** Activated automatically when Neo detects that the user’s prompt is too vague, or context is insufficient to proceed.

*   **Features:**
    
    *   Contains a **clarification prompt** that Neo fills out.
        
    *   Accepts direct text input and supports file uploads using the **paperclip icon**.
        
    *   Can also be **manually triggered** by the user or agent for branching logic.
        
    

> This node helps ensure clarity, especially when multi-step tasks require exact requirements before continuing.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FsNLRU7640iYjfe1uB8tw%252Fask_user_more.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D047aae0b-7b56-4be7-8dbe-92d9a8abfdee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=11ee560c&sv=2)

You can call the Ask User More tool by a simple prompt

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#recipe-nodes-and-task-control)

Recipe Nodes & Task Control


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#what-is-a-recipe-node)

What is a Recipe Node?

Recipe Nodes are the **elliptical step indicators** that appear between each major task block in the canvas. They represent the logical transition from one subtask to the next in Neo's active Recipe.

These nodes visually mark where Neo has paused to evaluate a result, shift context, or prepare for the next operation.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#functionality)

Functionality

**Restart from this point:** Hover over the node and click the **Refresh icon** to reinitialize Neo’s planning from this specific step in the Recipe.

*   **Contextual Rebuild:** When restarted, Neo regenerates the Recipe forward from this node using the latest outputs, edits, or external file uploads, without needing to rerun previous steps.
    

> This is useful for correcting logic paths or introducing new information without discarding prior work.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#when-to-use-it)

When to use it

*   You want to re-test from a specific step onward
    
*   You need to fix a failed task or broken output without starting over
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FN5MX6JwCrG1SqQmeksYV%252Frestart_task.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db828ecff-2cde-43a4-9ceb-a0e5b7355314&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa93be8a&sv=2)

Restart a Task from any Recipe Node

> Neo’s dynamic planning engine will respect the prior flow while adapting downstream logic, preserving the fluidity of the Recipe.

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#downloading-agent-files)

Downloading Agent Files


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#accessing-the-file-panel)

Accessing the File Panel

After Neo completes any file-based task — such as generating documents, webpages, or analysis — all resulting files are stored under the **Files panel** in the left sidebar.

*   **Click the** `**Files**` **button** (folder icon) to open the list of all downloadable items created during the current Recipe.
    

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#download-options)

Download Options

Once inside the Files panel, you have two options for retrieving Neo’s output:

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-1.-manual-review-and-download)

1\. Manual Review and Download

*   **Browse the file tree** to see all available items by title.
    
*   Each file is labeled with:
    
    *   A unique name based on the content or task
        
    *   A download count indicator (how many times it was revised or regenerated)
        
    
*   Click on any filename to **download it individually**.
    

> Use this method when you want to preview or selectively download results.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#id-2.-download-all-files-at-once)

2\. Download All Files at Once

*   Click the **Download All Files** icon (⇩) at the top-right of the Files panel.
    
*   This will **bundle all generated files into a single** `**.zip**` **archive** and initiate an immediate download.
    

> Ideal for exporting full project outputs, such as multiple reports, bundled HTML+CSS+JS files, or full document packs.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FUgoYbWL9Om9iB0fvhi17%252Fdownload_files.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ffccbb9-95ee-4d12-9033-0e581b6ddbed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9cb7885d&sv=2)

Download All Files Button Located Beside "Files generated by the Agent" text

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#how-to-create-new-branches-in-the-same-canvas)

How to Create New Branches in the Same Canvas


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Click on the "New Branch" button.
    
*   In the dialog box that appears at the bottom of the page, enter your new query or topic.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FUZSier34VM9mXed3xp2P%252FOracle-%25E4%25BD%25BF%25E7%2594%25A8%25E6%258C%2587%25E5%258D%2597-%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%2590%25AF%25E6%2596%25B0%25E5%2588%2586%25E6%2594%25AF-new-branch.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde99c89c-a8a5-4abe-bfbe-afb21e499fcf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7e83e24&sv=2)

You Can Host Multiple Branches in the Same Flow

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#sharing-a-flow)

Sharing a Flow


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#using-the-share-button)

Using the Share Button

To collaborate on or showcase your current Flow, use the `**Share**` **button** located at the top-left of the Canvas.

*   Click the `Share` button to generate a **unique Flow URL**.
    
*   This link allows others to view or join the session.
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252Fp85EY2lXUa7YedocuJbi%252Fshare_button.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbac9ac4-d4b4-456c-ad0e-5a4e7d39be31&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=92b8ee69&sv=2)

Only Grant Edit Permissions to Users You Trust

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#important-sharing-rules)

Important Sharing Rules

*   **Default Share Mode:** By default, sharing a Flow will **only grant view access to replies** — the recipient can see what Neo generated, but **cannot edit or interact** with the Recipe.
    
*   **Granting Edit Access:** After someone has joined using the shared link, you can **manually assign edit permissions** from the member management dropdown. Edit permissions must be granted for a user to view the contents of a Flow, or else they will only see the replay of the Flow
    

> Only collaborators with edit access can modify task inputs, rerun nodes, or inject new files into the session.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#swapping-to-regular-mode)

Swapping to Regular Mode

If you don’t need full Agent execution, you can switch to **Regular Mode** to prompt a specific model directly. This is ideal for fast responses, brainstorming, and comparisons

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/canvas-navigation-in-agent-mode#available-modes-in-regular-mode)

Available Modes in Regular Mode

**Regular (Prompt a Model)** Choose from available models (e.g., Claude, GPT, Gemini) and ask questions or generate text without triggering Agent Mode.

*   **Online Search** Send your prompt to a model with access to real-time web search. Choose which model will handle the query + summarization.
    
*   **Image / Video** Prompt any supported vision model for analysis, captioning, or enhancement suggestions.
    
*   **Prompt Enhance** Automatically rewrites your prompt to be more detailed, structured, or effective .
    
*   **Comparison Mode** Run the same prompt across multiple models side-by-side and compare their outputs in a unified view.
    

* * *

> Regular Mode is flexible, fast, and model-specific. Use it when you want direct control over how a prompt is handled—without planning or execution steps.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3690352926-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%252Fuploads%252FrIPEFMBRMmeA8KGtsQrY%252Fregular_mode_toggle.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f5078b0-96c9-43ca-8051-38c254c26cbd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9be15671&sv=2)

# About Oracle Mode | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FBOw5ufjnihpyHsRl6OPP%2F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82f401d1&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/about-oracle-mode#what-is-oracle)

**What is Oracle?**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Oracle is a cutting-edge intelligent agent system developed by the flowith team, designed with the goal of achieving pre-AGI (pre-Artificial General Intelligence). It is specifically engineered to handle multi-step, complex tasks that require the use of multiple tools.

Key features of Oracle include:

*   Autonomous task planning
    
*   Task decomposition
    
*   Unlimited tool utilization
    
*   Self-optimization
    

Oracle's external capabilities are continuously updated and upgraded, allowing it to become increasingly powerful over time.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FFe0YxPmfFaclcndbPzUc%2FAmazing%2520Mockups.jpeg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e138a96b&sv=2)

Oracle Recipe and Nodes

In other words, Oracle is a **data-level** (operating at the data layer, without physical medium or real-world interaction) **generalized** (capable of performing general tasks, not limited to pre-trained or pre-defined functions) **Agent** (beyond just an LLM, able to utilize tools, manage memory, and collaborate with multiple LLMs) that can complete complex tas**ks** (beyond simple queries or commands) and adapt to new situations (capable of self-learning and processing in novel environments or tasks).

[](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/about-oracle-mode#core-concepts)

**Core Concepts**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Recipe Workflow**

The term "recipe" originally refers to a set of instructions for preparing a dish. In the context of Oracle, a Recipe represents a systematic workflow that AI executes to complete user tasks. When a user inputs a requirement or instruction, Oracle breaks down the overall directive into smaller subtasks based on its capabilities and available tools. These subtasks are then passed to a task allocator for step-by-step execution.

After designing a complete Recipe, Oracle always confirms it with the user before beginning execution. During this confirmation process, users can directly modify specific steps within the Recipe, including:

*   Adjusting the order of steps
    
*   Deleting steps
    
*   Modifying text
    
*   Adding new steps
    

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2FBOw5ufjnihpyHsRl6OPP%2F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=82f401d1&sv=2)

A Recipe Generated by Oracle

**Dispatcher**

The Dispatcher, also known as a Task Allocator, is a crucial component in the execution of subtasks generated by the Oracle. For each Oracle-generated subtask, a dedicated Agent within the Dispatcher is responsible for allocation and implementation. This Agent identifies the most suitable tool from the Oracle's supported toolset and then executes and completes the subtask.

For example, when the subtask is "**search for user reviews of flowith on social media**", the task allocator will invoke the "**Twitter Search Tool**", "**Reddit Search Tool**", and "**Google Search Tool**" to conduct searches for Flowith user reviews.

You can view the currently supported tools for Oracle on the Oracle conversation initiation page. This list is updated in real-time, and we continuously add the most useful tools to Oracle's supported toolkit.

[Current Capabilities Supported by Oracle](https://doc.flowith.io/agent-mode-neo/current-capabilities-supported-by-oracle)

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FjTYyhELhBzd4Ov8Nl3WG%2Fblobs%2Ffef0NUW8zbPpdLgMeTJ5%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE4.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8e39647&sv=2)

Tools supported by Oracle

**Memory and Context Management**

Oracle is designed for complex tasks, which often generate extensive context due to their multi-step nature. If we were to provide all previous context to the LLM (Large Language Model), it could potentially impact its performance.

To address this, Oracle employs intelligent context management during task allocation and execution. For example, when Oracle reaches step 10 of a process, its memory manager evaluates which information from previous steps is essential and incorporates only the necessary context into the current step. This approach eliminates concerns about excessively long context.

**Self-Iteration and Update Recipe**

After completing each step, Oracle automatically updates the entire Recipe based on the execution results of each step. For instance, if it fails to find the required information, it will incorporate additional search steps into the subsequent stages to ensure successful task completion.

When Oracle inquires about user satisfaction with the results, and the user expresses dissatisfaction, it will generate additional steps in an attempt to provide the desired outcome.

Last updated 10 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Neo について | Flowith Official Document

![Page cover](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Fzu8C1nUY5LDCaMxYYNnm%2F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4dfcd71&sv=2)

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#what-is-agent-neo)

**What is Agent Neo?**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agent Neo is a cutting-edge intelligent agent designed by the Flowith team to autonomously handle complex, multi-step tasks. It represents an evolution beyond static, pre-planned execution agents, operating with a dynamic and adaptive methodology.

Key characteristics of Neo include:

*   **Autonomous:** Interprets high-level goals and works independently toward a solution.
    
*   **Dynamic:** Adapts its approach in real-time based on new information and the results of previous actions.
    
*   **Tool-Oriented:** Utilizes a diverse and expanding set of tools to gather information, process data, and execute actions.
    
*   **Self-Correcting:** Identifies failures or insufficient results and modifies its strategy to overcome obstacles and achieve the goal.
    

Neo's external capabilities are continuously updated and upgraded, allowing it to become increasingly powerful over time.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2FLb1TccN0scGPrEBlzdlD%2FAmazing%2520Mockups.jpeg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=50a313dc&sv=2)

Neo Recipe and Nodes

In other words, Neo is a **data-level** (operating at the data layer, without physical medium or real-world interaction) **generalized** (capable of performing general tasks, not limited to pre-trained or pre-defined functions) **Agent** (beyond just an LLM, able to utilize tools, manage memory, and collaborate with multiple LLMs) that can complete complex tas**ks** (beyond simple queries or commands) and adapt to new situations (capable of self-learning and processing in novel environments or tasks).

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#core-philosophy-from-static-plans-to-dynamic-recipes)

**Core Philosophy: From Static Plans to Dynamic Recipes**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The term "Recipe" originally refers to a set of instructions for preparing a dish. In the context of Neo, a Recipe represents a systematic workflow that AI executes to complete user tasks. When a user inputs a requirement or instruction, Neo breaks down the overall directive into smaller subtasks based on its capabilities and available tools. These subtasks are then passed to a task allocator for step-by-step execution.

> A **Recipe** is a living, evolving set of instructions that Neo builds and refines as it works, not just a fixed list created at the beginning. This dynamic approach is more effective for complex problems where the full path to a solution is not knowable in advance, allowing Neo to navigate uncertainty and adapt to new discoveries.

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Fzu8C1nUY5LDCaMxYYNnm%2F%25E4%25BA%25A712%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE%25205.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4dfcd71&sv=2)

A Recipe Generated by Neo

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#the-anatomy-of-a-neo-task-core-concept)

**The Anatomy of a Neo Task: Core Concept**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#the-dynamic-recipe-neos-evolving-strategy)

**The Dynamic Recipe: Neo's Evolving Strategy**

A Recipe is the real-time sequence of steps Neo executes. It is generated step-by-step during the task, with each new action informed by the outcome of the previous one. Users can monitor this process through a live execution log, which provides transparency into Neo's "thought process" as it happens.

The flow is cyclical and adaptive:

Goal -> First Step -> Execution -> Result Analysis -> Next Step -> ... -> Completion

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#the-dispatcher-and-tools-neos-capabilities)

**The Dispatcher & Tools: Neo's Capabilities**

The Dispatcher, also known as a Task Allocator, is a crucial component in the execution of subtasks generated by Neo. For each Neo-generated subtask, a dedicated Agent within the Dispatcher is responsible for allocation and implementation. This Agent identifies the most suitable tool from Neo's supported toolset and then executes and completes the subtask.

For example, when the subtask is "**search for user reviews of flowith on social media**", the task allocator will invoke the "**online\_search**" and "**read\_single\_webpage**" to conduct searches for Flowith user reviews.

You can view the currently supported tools for Neo on the Neo conversation initiation page. This list is updated in real-time, and we continuously add the most useful tools to Oracle's supported toolkit.

[Oracle がサポートする現在の機能](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/oracle-gasaptosuruno)

![](https://doc.flowith.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F2agAjJERs7Y6IiotYFD6%2Fblobs%2Fg6n2Kda04BzP3TPTHtPJ%2F%25E4%25BA%25A7%25E5%2593%2581%25E5%259B%25BE4.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebd383ce&sv=2)

Tools supported by Neo

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#intelligent-context-and-memory-management)

**Intelligent Context & Memory Management**

Complex tasks often generate extensive context. To maintain efficiency and accuracy, Neo employs an intelligent memory manager. For each step, the manager evaluates which information from previous steps is essential and injects only the necessary context. This prevents context overload and ensures the Large Language Model (LLM) can focus on the most relevant data for the current subtask.

### 

[](https://doc.flowith.io/flowith-heyoukoso/oracle-mdo-agent-mdo/neo-nitsuite#adaptation-and-self-correction)

**Adaptation and Self-Correction**

Neo's ability to self-correct is central to its power. The entire Recipe is fluid and can be altered mid-execution based on real-time results. This adaptation is triggered automatically by events such as:

*   **Tool Failure:** If a tool returns an error or no results, Neo will automatically try a different tool or rephrase its query.
    
*   **Unsatisfactory Results:** If the information gathered is insufficient, Neo will autonomously add new steps to find more data.
    
*   **New Discoveries:** Information found in one step can completely change the subsequent steps in the Recipe.
    

> **Example of Adaptation:**
> 
> 1.  **Goal:** "Summarize recent AI hardware announcements."
>     
> 2.  **Step 1:** Neo uses
>     
>     Google Search
>     
>     for "AI hardware announcements 2025".
>     
> 3.  **Result:** Results are mixed, including news articles and one press release for a "Project Chimera" chip.
>     
> 4.  **Adaptation:** Neo identifies "Project Chimera" as a key term and creates a new sub-task to investigate it.
>     
> 5.  **Step 2:** Neo performs a new, targeted search for
>     
>     "Project Chimera" chip specifications
>     

Last updated 1 month ago
